\left\lbrack \begin{matrix} {\sigma }_{r} & {\sigma }_{\theta r} & {\sigma }_{zr} \\ {\sigma }_{r\theta } & {\sigma }_{\theta } & {\sigma }_{z\theta } \\ {\sigma }_{rz} & {\sigma }_{\theta z} & {\sigma }_{z} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \sin \theta & 0 & \cos \theta \\ \cos \theta & 0 & - \sin \theta \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} {\sigma }_{11} & {\sigma }_{21} & {\sigma }_{31} \\ {\sigma }_{12} & {\sigma }_{22} & {\sigma }_{32} \\ {\sigma }_{13} & {\sigma }_{23} & {\sigma }_{33} \end{array}\right\rbrack \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \sin \theta & \cos \theta & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 1 \\ \cos \theta & - \sin \theta & 0 \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

16. 已知物体内某点的应力状态以直角坐标系表示时的应力张量为 ${\sigma }_{ji}$ . 试求以球坐标系表示时的应力张量.

答案: 其矩阵表示为

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{matrix} {\sigma }_{r} & {\sigma }_{\theta r} & {\sigma }_{\theta r} \\ {\sigma }_{r\theta } & {\sigma }_{\theta } & {\sigma }_{\theta \varphi } \\ {\sigma }_{r\varphi } & {\sigma }_{\theta \varphi } & {\sigma }_{\varphi } \end{matrix}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \sin \theta \cos \varphi & \sin \theta \sin \varphi & \cos \theta \\ \cos \theta \cos \varphi & \cos \theta \sin \varphi & - \sin \theta \\ - \sin \varphi & \cos \varphi & 0 \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} {\sigma }_{11} & {\sigma }_{21} & {\sigma }_{31} \\ {\sigma }_{12} & {\sigma }_{22} & {\sigma }_{32} \\ {\sigma }_{13} & {\sigma }_{23} & {\sigma }_{33} \end{array}\right\rbrack \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \sin \theta \cos \varphi & \cos \theta \cos \varphi & - \sin \varphi \\ \sin \theta \sin \varphi & \cos \theta \sin \varphi & \cos \varphi \\ \cos \theta & - \sin \theta & 0 \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

17. 试证明下列应力分量满足平衡方程 (设体力为零):

(1) ${\sigma }_{11} = Q\sin a{x}_{1}\operatorname{ch}a{x}_{2}$ ,

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = - Q\sin a{x}_{1}\operatorname{ch}a{x}_{2},
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = - Q\cos a{x}_{1}\operatorname{sh}a{x}_{2}.
$$

(2) ${\sigma }_{11} = \sin a{x}_{1}\left( {2{c}_{2} + 6{c}_{3}{x}_{2} + {12}{c}_{4}{x}_{2}^{2} + \cdots }\right)$ ,

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = - {a}^{2}\sin a{x}_{1}\left( {{c}_{0} + {c}_{1}{x}_{2} + {c}_{2}{x}_{2}^{2} + {c}_{3}{x}_{2}^{3} + {c}_{4}{x}_{2}^{4} + \cdots }\right) ,
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = - a\cos a{x}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1} + 2{c}_{2}{x}_{2} + 3{c}_{3}{x}_{2}^{2} + 4{c}_{4}{x}_{2}^{3} + \cdots }\right) .
$$

式中, $Q\text{、}a\text{、}{c}_{0}\text{、}{c}_{1}\text{、}\cdots$ 均为常数.

18. 已知处于平衡状态的平板上 (图 2-13) 的应力分量为 ${\sigma }_{11} = q{x}_{1}{x}_{2},{\sigma }_{22} = 0,{\sigma }_{12} = c\left( {\frac{{h}^{2}}{4} - {x}_{2}^{2}}\right)$ . 试求出系数 $c$ ,并在板面上画出 ${x}_{1} = l$ 处的应力分布 (体力为零).

## 第 3 章

## 应变分析

在静力学中,当物体内某点的应力张量 ${\sigma }_{ji}$ 为已知时,则该点的应力状态即被确定, 可见应力张量是求解物体受力问题的关键. 然而, 第 2 章中并没有涉及应力张量的求解问题. 因为在一般情况下, 一点的应力张量往往是根据物体受力与变形的关系通过间接测量计算出来的. 此外, 从动力学观点看, 运动微分方程是连接应力张量、体力分量和位移函数的偏微分方程. 欲对其求解, 必须建立位移与形变、形变与应力之间的关系. 因此, 有必要对物体的变形问题作进一步的讨论, 为最终求解应力张量和运动方程奠定基础.

## 3.1 位 移 场

设正交坐标系 ${x}_{i}$ 中有一物体 $V$ ,在外载作用下物体发生位置的改变和变形, 使 $V$ 变成 ${V}^{\prime }$ (图 3-1), $V$ 内任一点 $A\left( r\right)$ 移到了 ${A}^{\prime }\left( {r}^{\prime }\right)$ 点. 因为构成 $V$ 与 ${V}^{\prime }$ 的质点是一一对应的,因此 ${\mathbf{r}}^{\prime }$ 应是 $r$ 的单值连续函数. 可以写成

$$
{\mathbf{r}}^{\prime } = {\mathbf{r}}^{\prime }\left( r\right) \tag{3.1}
$$

物体 $V$ 到 ${V}^{\prime }$ 的位移场为

$$
\mathbf{u}\left( r\right) = {\mathbf{r}}^{\prime }\left( r\right) - \mathbf{r} \tag{3.2}
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_51_536_1528_681_443_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_51_536_1528_681_443_0-20241011170328-m597dzj.jpg)

图 3-1

由此,位移场 $\mathbf{u}\left( r\right)$ 也是径向 $r$ 的单值连续函数.

设物体内有 $A$ 点,在其极近处有 $B$ 点, ${AB} = \mathrm{d}r$ . 在外来作用下, $A$ 点移至 ${A}^{\prime }$ 点, $B$ 点移至 ${B}^{\prime }$ 点, ${A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime } = \mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }.A\text{、}B$ 的位移可分别设为 $u\left( r\right)$ 和 $u\left( {r + \mathrm{d}r}\right)$ . 若将其用哑指标表示, 则有

$$
u\left( r\right) \Rightarrow {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right)
$$

$$
\mathbf{u}\left( {r + \mathrm{d}r}\right) \Rightarrow {u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) \tag{3.3}
$$

由于 $B$ 点十分接近 $A$ 点, $\mathrm{d}r$ 为一阶无穷小量. 故对 ${u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right)$ 进行泰勒展开只取一次项, 有

$$
{u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) = {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) + \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j} \tag{3.4}
$$

将等式右端加、减 $\frac{1}{2}\frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}$ 项,得

$$
{u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) = {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) + \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{j} + \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} - \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{j} \tag{3. 5}
$$

令

$$
{e}_{ji} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right) \tag{3. 6}
$$

$$
{\omega }_{ji} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} - \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right) \tag{3.7}
$$

则式(3.5)成为

$$
{}^{\prime \prime }{u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) = {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) + {e}_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j} + {\omega }_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j} \tag{3.8}
$$

称 ${e}_{ji}$ 为应变张量, ${\omega }_{ji}$ 为旋转张量. 其展开式为

$$
{e}_{11} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}},\;{e}_{12} = {e}_{21} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}\right)
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}},\;{e}_{23} = {e}_{32} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}}}\right) \tag{3.9}
$$

$$
{e}_{33} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}},\;{e}_{31} = {e}_{13} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}\right)
$$

$$
{\omega }_{11} = 0,\;{\omega }_{12} = - {\omega }_{21} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} - \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}}\right) = \left( {\omega }_{3}\right)
$$

$$
{\omega }_{22} = 0,\;{\omega }_{23} = - {\omega }_{32} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}} - \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}}}\right) = \left( {\omega }_{1}\right) \tag{3.10}
$$

$$
{\omega }_{33} = 0,\;{\omega }_{31} = - {\omega }_{13} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}} - \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}\right) = \left( {\omega }_{2}\right)
$$

由此可知,应变张量为对称张量,旋转张量为反对称张量.

式(3.8)还可写成矩阵形式, 即(3. 11)

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_53_214_333_1275_175_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_53_214_333_1275_175_0-20241011170328-so89k80.jpg)

对于应变问题,如果弄清 $A\text{、}B$ 两点的位移,即可判断 ${AB}$ 线段的变形情况,由此可见, ${e}_{ji}$ 与 ${\omega }_{ji}$ 是描述物体变形的物理量.

## 3.2 应变张量、旋转张量

## 3. 2.1 应变张量

## 1. 对角元素的讨论

由图 3-1 知,当 $\mathbf{r}$ 用 ${x}_{i}$ 表示, ${\mathbf{r}}^{\prime }$ 用 ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 表示时, ${x}_{i}$ 与 ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 之间存在如下关系:

$$
{x}_{i}^{\prime } = {x}_{i} + {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) \tag{3. 12}
$$

两边微分, 得

$$
\mathrm{d}{x}_{i}^{\prime } = \mathrm{d}{x}_{i} + \mathrm{d}{u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) \;\left\lbrack {\text{ 以下省略 }\left( {x}_{j}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

两边平方, 有

$$
{\left( \mathrm{d}{x}_{i}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = {\left( \mathrm{d}{x}_{i}\right) }^{2} + 2\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{i}\mathrm{\;d}{u}_{i} + {\left( \mathrm{d}{u}_{i}\right) }^{2}
$$

由于 ${\left( \mathrm{d}{u}_{i}\right) }^{2}$ 为二阶无穷小量,故可省略. 且 ${\left( \mathrm{d}{x}_{i}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = {\left( \mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }\right) }^{2},{\left( \mathrm{d}{x}_{i}\right) }^{2} = {\left( \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2}$ ,所以有

$$
{\left( \mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = {\left( \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2} + 2\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{i}\mathrm{\;d}{u}_{i} \tag{3. 13}
$$

因为 ${u}_{i}$ 是 ${x}_{j}$ 的单值连续函数,故有 $\mathrm{d}{u}_{i} = \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}$ ,代入得

$$
{\left( \mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = {\left( \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2} + 2\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{i} \tag{3.14}
$$

利用哑指标规则 3 , 有

$$
{\left( \mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = {\left( \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2} + \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{i} = {\left( \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2} + 2{e}_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{i} \tag{3. 15}
$$

两边同除 ${\left( \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2}$ ,得

$$
{\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }}{\mathrm{d}r}\right) }^{2} = 1 + 2{e}_{ji}\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}{\mathrm{\;d}r}\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{i}}{\mathrm{\;d}r}
$$

因为 $\mathrm{d}r$ 为 $\mathrm{d}{x}_{j}\text{、}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{i}$ 的模值,所以有 $\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {n}_{j},\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{i}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {n}_{i}$ ,代入得

$$
{\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }}{\mathrm{d}r}\right) }^{2} = 1 + 2{e}_{ji}{n}_{j}{n}_{i} \tag{3.16}
$$

同前相仿,在等式右端再加一个二阶无穷小量 ${e}_{ji}^{2}{n}_{j}^{2}{n}_{i}^{2}$ ,则有

$$
{\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime }}{\mathrm{d}r}\right) }^{2} = {\left( 1 + {e}_{ji}{n}_{j}{n}_{i}\right) }^{2} \tag{3. 17}
$$

整理得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime } - \mathrm{d}r}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {e}_{ji}{n}_{j}{n}_{i} \tag{3. 18}
$$

很明显, $\left( {\mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime } - \mathrm{d}r}\right) /\mathrm{d}r$ 为 $\mathrm{d}r$ 的相对伸长量,即线应变. 可用 ${e}_{r}$ 表示,则

$$
{e}_{r} = {e}_{ji}{n}_{j}{n}_{i} \tag{3.19}
$$

展开后得

$$
{e}_{r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{1}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{2}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{3}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{1}{n}_{2} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{2}{n}_{3} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{1}{n}_{3} \tag{3.20}
$$

利用该式,很容易看出应变张量对角元素的物理意义. 当线元 $\mathrm{d}r$ 原来在 ${x}_{1}$ 方向时,则 ${n}_{1} = 1,{n}_{2} = {n}_{3} = 0$ ,因此有

$$
{e}_{r1} = {e}_{11} \tag{3. 21}
$$

同理,当线元 $\mathrm{d}r$ 原来在 ${x}_{2}\text{、}{x}_{3}$ 方向上时,可得

$$
{e}_{r2} = {e}_{22}
$$

$$
{e}_{r3} = {e}_{33} \tag{3.22}
$$

很明显, ${e}_{r1}\text{、}{e}_{r2}\text{、}{e}_{r3}$ 是 ${x}_{1}\text{、}{x}_{2}\text{、}{x}_{3}$ 方向上的线段沿各自方向的线应变或相对伸长量. 由此可见,应变张量的对角元素 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}\text{、}{e}_{33}$ 分别表示与 ${x}_{1}\text{、}{x}_{2}\text{、}{x}_{3}$ 平行的线段在各自方向上的相对伸长量.

## 2. 非对角元素的讨论

在 3.1 节的讨论中, ${u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right)$ 为 $B$ 点的位移, ${u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right)$ 为 $A$ 点的位移,根据泰勒展开有

$$
{u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) = {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) + \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j} \tag{3.23}
$$

如果线元 ${AB}$ 在变形前沿 ${x}_{1}$ 方向,则 $A$ 点的位置为 $\left( {{x}_{1},0,0}\right) , B$ 点的位置为 $\left( {{x}_{1} + }\right.$ $\left. {\mathrm{d}{x}_{1},0,0}\right)$ . 此时式 (3.23) 成为

$$
{u}_{1}\left( {{x}_{1} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}}\right) - {u}_{1}\left( {x}_{1}\right) = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{1}
$$

$$
{u}_{2}\left( {{x}_{1} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}}\right) - {u}_{2}\left( {x}_{1}\right) = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{1} \tag{3.24}
$$

$$
{u}_{3}\left( {{x}_{1} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}}\right) - {u}_{3}\left( {x}_{1}\right) = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{1}
$$

同样,如果线元 ${AB}$ 变形前沿 ${x}_{2}$ 方向,则有

$$
{u}_{1}\left( {{x}_{2} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{2}}\right) - {u}_{1}\left( {x}_{2}\right) = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2}
$$

$$
{u}_{2}\left( {{x}_{2} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{2}}\right) - {u}_{2}\left( {x}_{2}\right) = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2} \tag{3.25}
$$

$$
{u}_{3}\left( {{x}_{2} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{2}}\right) - {u}_{3}\left( {x}_{2}\right) = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2}
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_55_232_458_568_393_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_55_232_458_568_393_0-20241011170328-3fkco19.jpg)

图 3-2

如图 3-2 所示, $\mathrm{d}{x}_{1}\left( {AB}\right)$ 即为变形前沿 ${x}_{1}$ 方向的线元, $\mathrm{d}{x}_{2}\left( {AC}\right)$ 为变形前沿 ${x}_{2}$ 方向的线元. 变形后 ${AB}$ 成为 ${A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime }$ , ${AC}$ 成为 ${A}^{\prime }{C}^{\prime },\Delta {\theta }_{1}$ 表示线元 ${AB}$ 变形后的角度改变量, ${\Delta \theta }$ 表示线元 ${AC}$ 变形后的角度改变量. 由图 3-2 中三角形 ${A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime }{B}^{\prime }$ 可知

$$
\tan \Delta {\theta }_{1} = \frac{{B}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime }}{{A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime }} \tag{3.26}
$$

对于小变形而言, $\Delta {\theta }_{1}$ 很小,故有

$$
\Delta {\theta }_{1} = \frac{{B}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime }}{{A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime }} \tag{3. 27}
$$

式中,

$$
{A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime } = \mathrm{d}{x}_{1} + {e}_{11}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{1} = \left( {1 + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}
$$

$$
{B}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime \prime } = {u}_{2}\left( {{x}_{1} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}}\right) - {u}_{2}\left( {x}_{1}\right) = \left( \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}
$$

于是

$$
\Delta {\theta }_{1} = \frac{\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}{\left( 1 + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\right) }
$$

$\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}$ 表示 ${AB}$ 在 ${x}_{1}$ 方向上的相对伸长,它比 1 小得多,故可略去,于是上式成为

$$
\Delta {\theta }_{1} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} \tag{3. 28}
$$

同样, 可求得

$$
{\Delta \theta } = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} \tag{3.29}
$$

从而有

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}\right) = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{\Delta \theta } + \Delta {\theta }_{1}}\right) \tag{3.30}
$$

根据第 1 章中所讲的剪应变定义可知, ${e}_{12}$ (或 ${e}_{21}$ ) 为 $O{x}_{1}{x}_{2}$ 平面内的剪应变. 同理, 可证明 ${e}_{23}$ (或 ${e}_{32}$ ) 为 $O{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ 平面内的剪应变, ${e}_{31}$ (或 ${e}_{13}$ ) 为 $O{x}_{1}{x}_{3}$ 平面内的剪应变.

由此可见, 在应变张量的 9 个分量中, 对角线元素分别表示物体沿各坐标轴方向上的线应变, 而非对角线元素则分别表示与各坐标平面平行的面上的剪应变.

## 3. 2.2 旋转张量

由 ${e}_{12}$ 的讨论可知

$$
{\omega }_{12} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} - \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}}\right) = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\Delta {\theta }_{1} - {\Delta \theta }}\right) \tag{3. 31}
$$

即 ${\omega }_{12}$ 是 $O{x}_{1}{x}_{2}$ 平面两条相互垂直的线段变形以后角度改变之差的 $1/2$ 倍. 同理 ${\omega }_{23}$ 是 $O{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ 平面两条相互垂直的线段变形后角度改变之差的 $1/2$ 倍, ${\omega }_{31}$ 是 $O{x}_{1}{x}_{3}$ 平面两条相互垂直的线段变形后角度改变之差的 $1/2$ 倍. ${\omega }_{12}\text{、}{\omega }_{23}\text{、}{\omega }_{31}$ 反映了物体变形过程中宏观旋转状态的情况.

因此, 对于式 (3.8)

$$
{u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) = {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) + {e}_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j} + {\omega }_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}
$$

且作如下解释: 任一线段的位移可以表示为平动位移 ${u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right)$ 、形变位移 ${e}_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}$ 以及旋转位移 ${\omega }_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}$ 的和.

## 3. 3 一点的应变状态

利用式(3.4)

$$
{u}_{i}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) = {u}_{i}\left( {x}_{j}\right) + \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{j}
$$

当 $i$ 取 1 时, ${u}_{1}\left( {x}_{j}\right)$ 表示 $A$ 点的位移在 ${x}_{1}$ 轴方向上的投影 (图 3-3), ${u}_{1}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right)$ 表示 $B$ 点的位移在 ${x}_{1}$ 轴方向上的投影. 由图 3-3 可以看出, ${u}_{1}\left( {{x}_{j} + \mathrm{d}{x}_{j}}\right) -$ ${u}_{1}\left( {x}_{j}\right)$ 是线段 $\mathrm{d}r$ 的改变量 $\mathrm{d}{r}^{\prime } - \mathrm{d}r$ 在 ${x}_{1}$ 轴上的投影. 它包含着线量伸长与角量改变的综合成分,若增量为 $\delta {u}_{1}$ ,则由式 (3.4) 可得

$$
\delta {u}_{1} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{1} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{3} \tag{3.32}
$$

根据应变的定义,可知 $\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\mathrm{\;d}r}$ 的意义为线段 $\mathrm{d}r$ 由线量伸长 (线应变) 与角量改变 (剪应变) 而引起的 “总”的形变在 ${x}_{1}$ 轴方向上的投影,若以 ${e}_{r1}$ 表示,则有

$$
{e}_{r1} = \frac{\delta {u}_{1}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{1}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{2}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{3}}{\mathrm{\;d}r}
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_57_568_246_612_455_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_57_568_246_612_455_0-20241011170328-htnjli1.jpg)

图 3-3

因为 $\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{1}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {n}_{1},\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{2}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {n}_{2},\frac{\mathrm{d}{x}_{3}}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {n}_{3}$ ,所以上式可变为

$$
{e}_{r1} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{3} \tag{3.33}
$$

同理,若以 ${e}_{r2}\text{、}{e}_{r3}$ 表示 “总”的形变在 ${x}_{2}\text{、}{x}_{3}$ 轴方向上的投影,则可得式 (3.34) 中的后两式, 即

$$
{e}_{r1} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{3}
$$

$$
{e}_{r2} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{3} \tag{3.34}
$$

$$
{e}_{r3} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{3}
$$

式 (3.34) 就是 “总”的形变在各坐标轴上分量的数学表示式. 其哑指标形式为

$$
{e}_{ri} = \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}{n}_{j} \tag{3. 35}
$$

其矩阵形式为

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{l} {e}_{r1} \\ {e}_{r2} \\ {e}_{r3} \end{array}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \\ \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \\ \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \end{array}\right\rbrack \left\lbrack \begin{array}{l} {n}_{1} \\ {n}_{2} \\ {n}_{3} \end{array}\right\rbrack \tag{3. 36}
$$

式中,

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \\ \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \\ \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \end{array}\right\rbrack \tag{3. 37}
$$

称为相对位移张量. 它可以分解为应变张量与旋转张量, 即

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \\ \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \\ \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}} & \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \end{array}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} {e}_{11} & {e}_{21} & {e}_{31} \\ {e}_{12} & {e}_{22} & {e}_{32} \\ {e}_{13} & {e}_{23} & {e}_{33} \end{array}\right\rbrack + \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} 0 & - {\omega }_{3} & {\omega }_{2} \\ {\omega }_{3} & 0 & - {\omega }_{1} \\ - {\omega }_{2} & {\omega }_{1} & 0 \end{matrix}\right\rbrack \tag{3. 38}
$$

由上面讨论可以看出: 表现 “总”的应变在各坐标轴上分量的式 (3.36) 与第 2 章中表现总应力在各坐标轴上分量的式 (2.8) 完全相似, 不同的只是相对位移张量不是对称张量. 因为在一般情况下, $\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}} \neq \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}},\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}} \neq \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}},\frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}} \neq \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}$ ,而应力张量是对称张量.

与讨论应力问题一样,下面我们讨论图 3-3 中线段 ${AB}\left( {\mathrm{\;d}r}\right)$ 的正应变与剪应变.

由于 ${AB}$ 线段 “总” 的应变在各坐标轴上的投影为 ${e}_{r1}\text{、}{e}_{r2}\text{、}{e}_{r3}$ ,而 ${AB}$ 的正应变应该是 ${AB}$ 原方向上的线应变. 将 ${e}_{r1}\text{、}{e}_{r2}\text{、}{e}_{r3}$ 投影在 ${AB}$ 的原方向上,即得 ${AB}$ 线段的正应变,若以 ${e}_{r}$ 表示,则应有

$$
{e}_{r} = {e}_{r1}{n}_{1} + {e}_{r2}{n}_{2} + {e}_{r3}{n}_{3} \tag{3.39}
$$

将 ${e}_{n}$ 代入得

$$
{e}_{r} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1}^{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{1}{n}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{1}{n}_{3} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1}{n}_{2} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{2}^{2}
$$

$$
+ \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{2}{n}_{3} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}}{n}_{1}{n}_{3} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}}{n}_{2}{n}_{3} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}}{n}_{3}^{2}
$$

考虑到式(3.9), 则有

$$
{e}_{r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{1}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{2}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{3}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{1}{n}_{2} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{2}{n}_{3} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{1}{n}_{3} \tag{3.40}
$$

很明显, 式 (3.40) 与式 (3.20) 完全相同, 而式 (3.20) 的意义是线段变形前后的相对伸长量 (线应变), 它并没有涉及线段是否旋转的问题. 对应图 3-3 来说, 相当于 ${D}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime }/{A}^{\prime }{D}^{\prime }$ ,在小变形的情况下,也就是当 ${\Delta \theta }$ 很小时,线段沿 ${A}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime }$ 方向上的线应变与线段 ${AB}$ 方向上的线应变值近似相等,故在忽略二阶无穷小量情况下进行推导,便得到两个完全相同的等式.

对于 ${AB}$ 线段的剪应变 (指某一线段的剪应变,不是通常定义的剪应变) 来说, 可由 “总”的应变、正应变以及剪应变 $\left( {\Delta \theta }\right)$ 各自产生的绝对位移 ${B}^{\prime }{C}^{\prime }\text{、}{D}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime }\text{、}{C}^{\prime }{D}^{\prime }$ 之间的关系求得. 从上面的讨论可以看出, 对于小变形而言, 可认为图 3-3 中的 ${D}^{\prime }{C}^{\prime } \bot {D}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime }$ ,且

$$
{D}^{\prime }{C}^{\prime } = {\Delta \theta }\mathrm{d}r
$$

$$
{D}^{\prime }{B}^{\prime } = {e}_{r}\mathrm{\;d}r
$$

$$
{B}^{\prime }{C}^{\prime } = {\left\lbrack {\left( {e}_{r1}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2} + {\left( {e}_{r2}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2} + {\left( {e}_{r3}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2}\right\rbrack }^{1/2}
$$

于是有

$$
{\left( \Delta \theta \mathrm{d}r\right) }^{2} + {\left( {e}_{r}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2} = {\left( {e}_{r1}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2} + {\left( {e}_{r2}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2} + {\left( {e}_{r3}\mathrm{\;d}r\right) }^{2}
$$

整理后得

$$
{\Delta \theta } = \sqrt{{e}_{r1}^{2} + {e}_{r2}^{2} + {e}_{r3}^{2} - {e}_{r}^{2}} \tag{3. 41}
$$

式(3.41) 即为求解任一线段剪应变的具体表示式. 读者可用此式验证例 1-4 的结果.

由以上讨论可以看出, 如果物体内某点的应变张量为已知, 那么该点的应变状态即被确定.

例 3-1 为测量平面应变分量 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}\text{、}{e}_{12}$ ,将 3 个电阻片贴在 ${x}_{1}$ 方向、与 ${x}_{1}$ 成 ${60}^{ \circ }$ 和 ${120}^{ \circ }$ 方向上[图 3-4(a)]. 测得该 3 个方向上的应变值为 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ . 试以 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ 表示 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}\text{、}{e}_{12}$ .

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_59_458_1262_827_289_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_59_458_1262_827_289_0-20241011170328-fz9zcrg.jpg)

图 3-4

解 题中所给测量应变值 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ 的装置叫做应变花,它由 3 个互成 ${60}^{ \circ }$ 角的电阻 (或其他感应器件) 应变计构成. 在地应力的测量中, 通常采用这类装置测量与地面平行的 3 个方向上的线应变 (或正应变), 并由此 3 个方向上的线应变求解该点的应变分量, 最后利用应力与应变的关系 (将在第 4 章讨论) 求解该点的应力分量.

常用的应变花有两种, 一种是本题所给的应变计成等角分布的等角应变花, 另一种是应变计成 ${45}^{ \circ }$ 角分布的直角应变花 [图 3-4(b)].

下面,我们根据本题的要求,求解平面应变分量 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}\text{、}{e}_{12}$ . 由于 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ 分别是 ${x}_{1}$ 方向、与 ${x}_{1}$ 成 ${60}^{ \circ }$ 角和 ${120}^{ \circ }$ 角方向上的正应变,且在 ${x}_{1}$ 方向上 ${n}_{1} = 1,{n}_{2} =$

${n}_{3} = 0$ ; 在与 ${x}_{1}$ 成 ${60}^{ \circ }$ 角的方向上 ${n}_{1} = 1/2,{n}_{2} = \sqrt{3}/2,{n}_{3} = 0$ ; 在与 ${x}_{1}$ 成 ${120}^{ \circ }$ 角的方向上 ${n}_{1} = - 1/2,{n}_{2} = \sqrt{3}/2,{n}_{3} = 0$ . 根据正应变的表示式 (3.40) 得

$$
{e}_{0} = {e}_{11}
$$

$$
{e}_{60} = {e}_{11}{\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + {e}_{22}{\left( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right) }^{2} + 2{e}_{12}\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) \left( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)
$$

$$
{e}_{120} = {e}_{11}{\left( -\frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + {e}_{22}{\left( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right) }^{2} + 2{e}_{12}\left( {-\frac{1}{2}}\right) \left( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)
$$

解此方程, 得

$$
{e}_{11} = {e}_{0}
$$

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{\left( {e}_{60} - {e}_{120}\right) }{\sqrt{3}}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = \frac{\left\lbrack 2\left( {e}_{60} + {e}_{120}\right) - {e}_{0}\right\rbrack }{3}
$$

上组式就是所求的以 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ 表示的平面应变分量.

## 3. 4 应变张量的坐标变换公式

如果正交坐标系 ${x}_{i}$ 中的 6 个应变分量为已知,则可求出对应于新正交坐标系 ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 中的 6 个应变分量. 为简单起见,我们使 ${x}_{i}$ 与 ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 坐标的原点重合. 如此, ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 便可看成是 ${x}_{i}$ 旋转而成. 它们之间的方向余弦如表 3-1 所示.

表 3-1

<div>
<table><thead><tr><th>变量</th><th>$ {x}_{1} $</th><th>$ {x}_{2} $</th><th>$ {x}_{3} $</th></tr></thead><tr><td>$ {x}_{1}^{\prime } $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{11} $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{12} $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{13} $</td></tr><tr><td>$ {x}_{2}^{\prime } $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{21} $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{22} $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{23} $</td></tr><tr><td>$ {x}_{3}^{\prime } $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{31} $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{32} $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{33} $</td></tr></table>
</div>

新坐标系与原坐标系的变换关系为

$$
{x}_{1}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{11}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{x}_{3}
$$

$$
{x}_{2}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{21}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{22}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{23}{x}_{3} \tag{3.42}
$$

$$
{x}_{3}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{31}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{32}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{33}{x}_{3}
$$

新坐标系与原坐标系中位移的变换关系为

$$
{u}_{1}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{11}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{u}_{3}
$$

$$
{u}_{2}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{21}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{22}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{23}{u}_{3} \tag{3.43}
$$

$$
{u}_{3}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{31}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{32}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{33}{u}_{3}
$$

这样一来, 新坐标系中的应变张量可表示为

$$
{e}_{11}^{\prime } = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{1}^{\prime }},\;{e}_{12}^{\prime } = {e}_{21}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{1}^{\prime }} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{2}^{\prime }}}\right)
$$

$$
{e}_{22}^{\prime } = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{2}^{\prime }},\;{e}_{23}^{\prime } = {e}_{32}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{3}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{2}^{\prime }} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{3}^{\prime }}}\right) \tag{3. 44}
$$

$$
{e}_{33}^{\prime } = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{3}^{\prime }},\;{e}_{31}^{\prime } = {e}_{13}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{1}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{3}^{\prime }} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{1}^{\prime }}}\right)
$$

因为 ${x}_{1}^{\prime }$ 可以看成是原坐标系中过原点 $O$ 的某一方向上的矢径,因此,应变分量中 ${e}_{11}^{\prime } = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{1}^{\prime }}$ 的意义为函数 ${u}_{1}^{\prime }$ 沿 ${x}_{1}^{\prime }$ 方向上的偏导数. 利用方向导数公式

$$
\frac{\partial f}{\partial l} = \cos \left( {l,{x}_{1}}\right) \frac{\partial f}{\partial {x}_{1}} + \cos \left( {l,{x}_{2}}\right) \frac{\partial f}{\partial {x}_{2}} + \cos \left( {l,{x}_{3}}\right) \frac{\partial f}{\partial {x}_{3}}
$$

得

$$
{e}_{11}^{\prime } = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{1}^{\prime }} = {\alpha }_{11}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{1}}\left( {{\alpha }_{11}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{u}_{3}}\right) + {\alpha }_{12}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{2}}\left( {{\alpha }_{11}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{u}_{3}}\right)
$$

$$
+ {\alpha }_{13}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{3}}\left( {{\alpha }_{11}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{u}_{3}}\right)
$$

$$
= {\alpha }_{11}^{2}\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} + {\alpha }_{12}^{2}\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} + {\alpha }_{13}^{2}\frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} + {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{12}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}}\right) + {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{13}
$$

$$
\times \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}}}\right) + {\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{13}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}}}\right)
$$

$$
= {\alpha }_{11}^{2}{e}_{11} + {\alpha }_{12}^{2}{e}_{22} + {\alpha }_{13}^{2}{e}_{33} + 2{\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{12}{e}_{12} + 2{\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{13}{e}_{13} + 2{\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{13}{e}_{23} \tag{3. {45}\mathrm{a}}
$$

同理得

$$
{e}_{22}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{21}^{2}{e}_{11} + {\alpha }_{22}^{2}{e}_{22} + {\alpha }_{23}^{2}{e}_{33} + 2{\alpha }_{21}{\alpha }_{22}{e}_{12} + 2{\alpha }_{22}{\alpha }_{23}{e}_{23} + 2{\alpha }_{21}{\alpha }_{23}{e}_{13} \tag{3. {45}\mathrm{\;b}}
$$

$$
{e}_{33}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{31}^{2}{e}_{11} + {\alpha }_{32}^{2}{e}_{22} + {\alpha }_{33}^{2}{e}_{33} + 2{\alpha }_{31}{\alpha }_{32}{e}_{12} + 2{\alpha }_{32}{\alpha }_{33}{e}_{23} + 2{\alpha }_{33}{\alpha }_{31}{e}_{31}
$$

利用坐标变换与方向导数公式,还可以求出 ${e}_{12}^{\prime }\text{、}{e}_{23}^{\prime }\text{、}{e}_{31}^{\prime }$ ,如

$$
{e}_{12}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{1}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}^{\prime }}{\partial {x}_{2}}}\right) = \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {\left( {{\alpha }_{11}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{1}} + {\alpha }_{12}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{2}} + {\alpha }_{13}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{3}}}\right) \left( {{\alpha }_{21}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{22}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{23}{u}_{3}}\right) }\right.
$$

$$
\left. {+\left( {{\alpha }_{21}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{1}} + {\alpha }_{22}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{2}} + {\alpha }_{23}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{3}}}\right) \left( {{\alpha }_{11}{u}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{u}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{u}_{3}}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{21}{e}_{11} + {\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{22}{e}_{22} + {\alpha }_{13}{\alpha }_{23}{e}_{33} + \left( {{\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{21} + {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{22}}\right) {e}_{12}
$$

$$
+ \left( {{\alpha }_{13}{\alpha }_{21} + {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{23}}\right) {e}_{13} + \left( {{\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{23} + {\alpha }_{13}{\alpha }_{22}}\right) {e}_{23} \tag{3. {46}\mathrm{a}}
$$

同理得

$$
{e}_{23}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{21}{\alpha }_{31}{e}_{11} + {\alpha }_{22}{\alpha }_{32}{e}_{22} + {\alpha }_{23}{\alpha }_{33}{e}_{33} + \left( {{\alpha }_{21}{\alpha }_{32} + {\alpha }_{22}{\alpha }_{31}}\right) {e}_{12}
$$

$$
+ \left( {{\alpha }_{22}{\alpha }_{33} + {\alpha }_{23}{\alpha }_{32}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{\alpha }_{23}{\alpha }_{31} + {\alpha }_{21}{\alpha }_{33}}\right) {e}_{31}
$$

$$
{e}_{31}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{31}{e}_{11} + {\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{32}{e}_{22} + {\alpha }_{13}{\alpha }_{33}{e}_{33} + \left( {{\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{32} + {\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{31}}\right) {e}_{12}
$$

$$
+ \left( {{\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{33} + {\alpha }_{13}{\alpha }_{32}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{\alpha }_{13}{\alpha }_{31} + {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{33}}\right) {e}_{31} \tag{3. {46}\mathrm{\;b}}
$$

式 (3.45)、式 (3.46) 中的 6 个分量就是坐标变换后的应变分量, 它可以写成如下的矩阵形式:(3. 47)

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_62_360_433_1015_182_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_62_360_433_1015_182_0-20241011170328-ck497ks.jpg)

也可写成哑指标形式

$$
{e}_{kl}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{kj}{\alpha }_{ii}{e}_{ji} \tag{3. 48}
$$

式(3.47)、式(3.48)称为应变张量的坐标变换公式.

## 3.5 主 应 变

如果某一方向上的线元变形以后只有相对伸长或相对缩短, 则该方向称为主方向. 其应变称为主应变,以 $e$ 表示.

由应变的讨论可知, 总的应变 (主方向上的) 与主应变在各坐标轴上的分量应该相等, 即

$$
{e}_{ri} - e{n}_{i} = 0 \tag{3. 49}
$$

由于

$$
{e}_{ri} = {e}_{ji}{n}_{j} + {\omega }_{ji}{n}_{j}
$$

且主方向上无旋转, 即旋转张量为零. 所以有

$$
{e}_{ji}{n}_{j} - e{n}_{i} = 0 \tag{3. 50}
$$

展开有

$$
\left( {{e}_{11} - e}\right) {n}_{1} + {e}_{21}{n}_{2} + {e}_{31}{n}_{3} = 0
$$

$$
{e}_{12}{n}_{1} + \left( {{e}_{22} - e}\right) {n}_{2} + {e}_{32}{n}_{3} = 0 \tag{3. 51}
$$

$$
{e}_{13}{n}_{1} + {e}_{23}{n}_{2} + \left( {{e}_{33} - e}\right) {n}_{3} = 0
$$

式中,

$$
{n}_{1}^{2} + {n}_{2}^{2} + {n}_{3}^{2} = 1
$$

欲使上述方程有 ${n}_{1}\text{、}{n}_{2}\text{、}{n}_{3}$ 不同时为零的解答,必有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \left( {{e}_{11} - e}\right) & {e}_{21} & {e}_{31} \\ {e}_{12} & \left( {{e}_{22} - e}\right) & {e}_{32} \\ {e}_{13} & {e}_{23} & \left( {{e}_{33} - e}\right) \end{matrix}\right| = 0
$$

展开并整理得

$$
{e}^{3} - {\theta }_{1}{e}^{2} + {\theta }_{2}e - {\theta }_{3} = 0 \tag{3. 52}
$$

式中,

$$
{\theta }_{1} = {e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}
$$

$$
{\theta }_{2} = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {e}_{11} & {e}_{12} \\ {e}_{21} & {e}_{22} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {e}_{22} & {e}_{23} \\ {e}_{32} & {e}_{33} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {e}_{33} & {e}_{31} \\ {e}_{13} & {e}_{11} \end{array}\right| \tag{3. 53}
$$

$$
{\theta }_{3} = \left| \begin{array}{lll} {e}_{11} & {e}_{21} & {e}_{31} \\ {e}_{12} & {e}_{22} & {e}_{32} \\ {e}_{13} & {e}_{23} & {e}_{33} \end{array}\right|
$$

式(3.52)称为求解主应变的特征方程式,式(3.53)中的 ${\theta }_{1}\text{、}{\theta }_{2}\text{、}{\theta }_{3}$ 分别称为应变张量的第一、第二、第三不变量. 与主应力问题的讨论相同, 式 (3.52) 有 3 个实根, 通常以 ${e}_{1}\text{、}{e}_{2}\text{、}{e}_{3}$ 表示,这就是所要求解的主应变.

若将所求得的主应变值 ${e}_{1}\text{、}{e}_{2}\text{、}{e}_{3}$ 代入式 (3.51),并考虑到 ${n}_{1}^{2} + {n}_{2}^{2} + {n}_{3}^{2} = 1$ ,便可求出对应 ${e}_{1}\text{、}{e}_{2}\text{、}{e}_{3}$ 的主方向 $\left( {{n}_{1},{n}_{2},{n}_{3}}\right) \text{、}\left( {{n}_{1}^{\prime },{n}_{2}^{\prime },{n}_{3}^{\prime }}\right) \text{、}\left( {{n}_{1}^{\prime \prime },{n}_{2}^{\prime \prime },{n}_{3}^{\prime \prime }}\right)$ . 与主应力的讨论过程完全相同,当 ${e}_{1} \neq {e}_{2} \neq {e}_{3}$ 时,有 ${n}_{i} \bot {n}_{i}^{\prime } \bot {n}_{i}^{\prime \prime }$ .

如果选用应变主轴为正交坐标系的 3 个坐标轴, 由于此时应变张量的非对角线元素都为零. 且 ${e}_{11} = {e}_{1},{e}_{22} = {e}_{2},{e}_{33} = {e}_{3}$ ,所以应变张量的不变量式 (3.53) 变为

$$
{\theta }_{1} = {e}_{1} + {e}_{2} + {e}_{3}
$$

$$
{\theta }_{2} = {e}_{1}{e}_{2} + {e}_{2}{e}_{3} + {e}_{3}{e}_{1} \tag{3. 54}
$$

$$
{\theta }_{3} = {e}_{1}{e}_{2}{e}_{3}
$$

例 3-2 设物体内某点的位移分量为

$$
{u}_{1} = {10} \times {10}^{-3} + {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {0.05} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{3},{u}_{2} = 5 \times {10}^{-3} - {0.05} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1} +
$$

${0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{2}{x}_{3},{u}_{3} = {1.0} \times {10}^{-3} - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ . 试求解点 $A\left( {1,1,1}\right)$ 的主应变.

解 首先由位移分量求解应变分量. 利用 ${e}_{ji} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right)$ ,得

$$
{e}_{11} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{2} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{3} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{33} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} = - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} = - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}/\partial {x}_{1} + \partial {u}_{1}/\partial {x}_{2}}{2} = {0.025} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{23} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}/\partial {x}_{2} + \partial {u}_{2}/\partial {x}_{3}}{2} = 0
$$

$$
{e}_{31} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}/\partial {x}_{3} + \partial {u}_{3}/\partial {x}_{1}}{2} = - {0.025} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

再利用应变分量求解应变张量的不变量, 即

$$
{\theta }_{1} = {e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{\theta }_{2} = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {e}_{11} & {e}_{12} \\ {e}_{21} & {e}_{22} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {e}_{22} & {e}_{23} \\ {e}_{32} & {e}_{33} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {e}_{33} & {e}_{31} \\ {e}_{13} & {e}_{11} \end{array}\right| = - {0.01125} \times {10}^{-6}
$$

$$
{\theta }_{3} = \left| \begin{array}{lll} {e}_{11} & {e}_{21} & {e}_{31} \\ {e}_{12} & {e}_{22} & {e}_{32} \\ {e}_{13} & {e}_{23} & {e}_{33} \end{array}\right| = - {0.001} \times {10}^{-9}
$$

将其代入特征方程式(3.52)得

$$
{e}^{3} - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{e}^{2} - {0.01125} \times {10}^{-6}e + {0.001} \times {10}^{-9} = 0
$$

为方便计算,令 ${10}^{4}e = x$ ,代入上式得

$$
{x}^{3} - {x}^{2} - {1.125x} + 1 = 0
$$

以 $x = y + 1/3$ 消去二次项得

$$
{y}^{3} - {1.46y} + {0.552} = 0
$$

此方程的根为

$$
{y}_{1} = {0.931}
$$

$$
{y}_{2} = {0.434}
$$

$$
{y}_{3} = - {1.364}
$$

还原后得

$$
{e}_{1} = {0.1264} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{2} = {0.0767} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{3} = - {0.1031} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

此便是所求解的主应变值. 如果将其分别代入式 (3.51) 并考虑到 ${n}_{1}^{2} + {n}_{2}^{2} + {n}_{3}^{2} = 1$ , 即可求得对应 ${e}_{1}\text{、}{e}_{2}\text{、}{e}_{3}$ 的主方向如下:

$$
\left( {-{0.724}, - {0.685},{0.080}}\right)
$$

$$
\left( {{0.679}, - {0.730}, - {0.094}}\right)
$$

$$
\left( {-{0.124},{0.015}, - {0.990}}\right)
$$

由此可见, 主应变的求解与主应力的求解完全对应.

## 3. 6 体积应变

设物体变形前体积为 $V$ ,变形后为 ${V}^{\prime }$ ,则体积应变定义为

$$
\theta = \frac{{V}^{\prime } - V}{V} \tag{3. 55}
$$

即体积应变为体积的相对改变量.

由于弹性力学所研究的物体均限于小变形物体,因此 ${e}_{ji}$ 应该是很小的量. 可以想象, 在这些小量当中, 非对角线元素 (角应变分量) 引起物体体积变形的量较之对角线元素 (线应变分量) 引起物体体积变形的量要小得多, 故在研究物体的体积应变时, 通常忽略由非对角线元素所引起的体积应变.

这样, 可以将坐标轴的取向平行于对角元素来进行体积应变的讨论. 设有一正平行六面微分体,其边长分别为 $\mathrm{d}{x}_{1}\text{、}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2}\text{、}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{3}$ ,如图 3-5(a) 所示,在变形前,它的体积是 $\mathrm{d}{x}_{1}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{3}$ ,在变形后[图 3-5(b)],它的体积成为 $\left( {1 + {e}_{11}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}\left( {1 + {e}_{22}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{2}$ $\left( {1 + {e}_{33}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{3}$ . 因此,体积应变为

$$
\theta = \frac{\left( {1 + {e}_{11}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}\left( {1 + {e}_{22}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{2}\left( {1 + {e}_{33}}\right) \mathrm{d}{x}_{3} - \mathrm{d}{x}_{1}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{3}}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{1}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{2}\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{3}}
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_65_328_782_1055_443_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_65_328_782_1055_443_0-20241011170328-67x7t56.jpg)

图 3-5

略去二阶小量并整理得

$$
\theta = {e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33} \tag{3. 56}
$$

这就是体积应变的数学表达式,若将 ${e}_{11} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}},{e}_{22} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}},{e}_{33} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}}$ 代入,得

$$
\theta = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} = \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{i}} \tag{3. 57}
$$

它给出了体积应变与位移之间的关系.

## 讨 论

## 三维地应变的测量

如前所述, 利用平面内三个方向上的正应变 (或线应变), 即可求出平面应变分量 (如例 3-1). 在实际问题中, 常常需要进行三维地应变的测量, 从而计算三维地应力. 目前, 所有测量地应力的方法中, 除水压致裂法直接进行的三维测量和超声波法进行的间接测量是利用地质体的强度、密度、波速改变等物理量进行测定外, 其余方法基本都与地应变的测量相关. 因此, 地应变测量是非常重要的.

在三维地应变测量中, 由于应变张量中有 6 个独立的分量, 所以需要有 6 个方程进行求解. 其原理与平面地应变测量相同, 具体方法是利用能够进行三维测量的应变计 (或其他方法) 测定空间确定的 6 个方向上的正应变 (或线应变), 然后利用正应变的表达式列方程组求解. 若设所测 6 个方向上的正应变分别为 ${e}_{1r}\text{、}{e}_{2r}\text{、}{e}_{3r}$ 、 ${e}_{4r}\text{、}{e}_{5r}\text{、}{e}_{6r}$ ,所对应的方向余弦为 ${n}_{1i}\text{、}{n}_{2i}\text{、}{n}_{3i}\text{、}{n}_{4i}\text{、}{n}_{5i}\text{、}{n}_{6i}$ . 则由式(3.40)得

$$
{e}_{1r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{11}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{12}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{13}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{11}{n}_{12} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{12}{n}_{13} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{13}{n}_{11}
$$

$$
{e}_{2r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{21}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{22}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{23}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{21}{n}_{22} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{22}{n}_{23} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{23}{n}_{21}
$$

$$
{e}_{3r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{31}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{32}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{33}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{31}{n}_{32} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{32}{n}_{33} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{33}{n}_{31}
$$

$$
{e}_{4r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{41}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{42}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{43}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{41}{n}_{42} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{42}{n}_{43} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{43}{n}_{41}
$$

$$
{e}_{5r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{51}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{52}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{53}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{51}{n}_{52} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{52}{n}_{53} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{53}{n}_{51}
$$

$$
{e}_{6r} = {e}_{11}{n}_{61}^{2} + {e}_{22}{n}_{62}^{2} + {e}_{33}{n}_{63}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}{n}_{61}{n}_{62} + 2{e}_{23}{n}_{62}{n}_{63} + 2{e}_{31}{n}_{63}{n}_{61}
$$

式中, ${e}_{1r}\text{、}{e}_{2r}\text{、}{e}_{3r}\text{、}{e}_{4r}\text{、}{e}_{5r}\text{、}{e}_{6r}$ 为可测量, ${n}_{1i}\text{、}{n}_{2i}\text{、}{n}_{3i}\text{、}{n}_{4i}\text{、}{n}_{5i}\text{、}{n}_{6i}$ 为由测量过程中几何关系确定的量,均可作为已知量. 于是解方程可得到应变分量 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}\text{、}{e}_{33}\text{、}{e}_{12}\text{、}{e}_{23}\text{、}{e}_{31}$ . 这就是所求的地应变张量. 它是进一步求解地应力的关键.

以上地应变的求解方法也可以推广至地应力的直接测量中去, 即利用 6 个方向上的正应力求解该点的应力张量的问题.

当然, 在实测问题中, 还会遇到这样或那样的问题, 应根据实际情况进行各种校正,使其达到应有的精度.

## 习题与参考答案

1. 简述应变张量、旋转张量中各分量的物理意义.
2. 已知位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = k\left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{20}}\right) ,{u}_{2} = - k\left( {{x}_{1} - {x}_{10}}\right)$ ,其中 $k\text{、}{x}_{10}\text{、}{x}_{20}$ 为已知常数. 试求应变分量及旋转分量, 并阐明此结果对应什么物理现象.
3. 设弹性物体中任意点的位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = {c}_{1}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {c}_{2}{x}_{3},{u}_{2} = {c}_{3}{x}_{1} + {c}_{4}{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ , ${u}_{3} = {c}_{5}{x}_{1}{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ . 试求应变张量与旋转张量.

答案: 其矩阵表示为

$$
\left\lbrack {e}_{ji}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} {c}_{1}{x}_{2} & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{1}{x}_{1} + {c}_{3}}\right) & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{5}{x}_{2}{x}_{3} + {c}_{2}}\right) \\ \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{1}{x}_{1} + {c}_{3}}\right) & {c}_{4}{x}_{3} & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{4}{x}_{2} + {c}_{5}{x}_{1}{x}_{3}}\right) \\ \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{5}{x}_{2}{x}_{3} + {c}_{2}}\right) & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{4}{x}_{2} + {c}_{5}{x}_{1}{x}_{3}}\right) & {c}_{5}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
\left\lbrack {\omega }_{ji}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} 0 & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{1}{x}_{1} - {c}_{3}}\right) & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{2} - {c}_{5}{x}_{2}{x}_{3}}\right) \\ \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{3} - {c}_{1}{x}_{1}}\right) & 0 & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{4}{x}_{2} - {c}_{5}{x}_{1}{x}_{3}}\right) \\ \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{5}{x}_{2}{x}_{3} - {c}_{2}}\right) & \frac{1}{2}\left( {{c}_{5}{x}_{1}{x}_{3} - {c}_{4}{x}_{2}}\right) & 0 \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

4. 已知位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = A{x}_{1}^{2} + B,{u}_{2} = B{x}_{2} + C{x}_{3}^{2},{u}_{3} = A{x}_{1} + B{x}_{2} + C{x}_{3}^{2}$ ,其中 $A\text{、}B\text{、}C$ 是常数. 试写出点 $P\left( {1,1,1}\right)$ 的应变张量、旋转张量、相对位移张量的矩阵表示式, 并验证式(3.38).
5. 如果位移分量可由一函数 $\varphi \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3}}\right)$ 导出,即 ${u}_{1} = \frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial {x}_{1}},{u}_{2} = \frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial {x}_{2}},{u}_{3} =$ $\frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial {x}_{3}}$ . 试证其旋转分量为零 (这种变形称为纯变形).
6. 已知由直角应变花测得的 3 个应变值为 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{45}\text{、}{e}_{90}$ . 试求该处与此应变花平行的平面上应变分量的数值.

答案: ${e}_{11} = {e}_{0},{e}_{22} = {e}_{90},{e}_{12} = {e}_{45} - \frac{\left( {e}_{0} + {e}_{90}\right) }{2}$ .

7. 已知物体内各点的位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = {\alpha }_{1}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{2}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{3}{x}_{3},{u}_{2} = {\beta }_{1}{x}_{1} + {\beta }_{2}{x}_{2} +$ ${\beta }_{3}{x}_{3},{u}_{3} = {\gamma }_{1}{x}_{1} + {\gamma }_{2}{x}_{2} + {\gamma }_{3}{x}_{3}$ ,式中 ${\alpha }_{i}\text{、}{\beta }_{i}\text{、}{\gamma }_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,3}\right)$ 均为常数. 试求任一与正交坐标轴成等角方向的线段的正应变.

答案: ${e}_{r} = \frac{1}{3}\left( {{\alpha }_{1} + {\alpha }_{2} + {\alpha }_{3} + {\beta }_{1} + {\beta }_{2} + {\beta }_{3} + {\gamma }_{1} + {\gamma }_{2} + {\gamma }_{3}}\right)$ .

8. 设物体内任意一点的位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = 5 \times {10}^{-4} + {0.1} \times {10}^{-4}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {0.05} \times$​${10}^{-4}{x}_{3},{u}_{2} = 3 \times {10}^{-4} - {0.05} \times {10}^{-4}{x}_{1} + {0.1} \times {10}^{-4}{x}_{2}{x}_{3},{u}_{3} = 2 \times {10}^{-4} - {0.1} \times$​${10}^{-4}{x}_{1}{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ ,试求解点 $A\left( {{0.5}, - 1,0}\right)$ 的主应变及主方向.

答案: 主应变为 ${e}_{1} = {0.0823} \times {10}^{-4},{e}_{2} = {0.0287} \times {10}^{-4},{e}_{3} = - {0.1045} \times {10}^{-4}$ ; 主方向为 $\left( {-{0.116},{0.512}, - {0.852}}\right)$ ; $\left( {{0.173},{0.854},{0.491}}\right)$ ; $( - {0.980}, - {0.083}$ , $- {0.185})$ .

9. 物体内一点的应变分量为 ${e}_{11} = {0.15} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{22} = - {0.04} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{33} = 0$ , ${e}_{12} = 0,{e}_{23} = {0.06} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{31} = 0$ . 试计算主应变及主方向.

答案: ${e}_{1} = {0.15} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{2} = {0.043} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{3} = - {0.083} \times {10}^{-3};\left( {1,0,0}\right) ;(0$ , ${0.585},{0.811});\left( {0, - {0.811},{0.585}}\right)$ .

10. 试写出在平面应变 $\left( {{e}_{33} = {e}_{23} = {e}_{31} = 0}\right)$ 情况下应变张量的不变量及主应变的表示式.

答案: ${\theta }_{1} = {e}_{11} + {e}_{22},\;{\theta }_{2} = {e}_{11}{e}_{22} - {e}_{12}^{2},\;{\theta }_{3} = 0$ ;

$$
{e}_{1},{e}_{2} = \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {\left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) \pm \sqrt{{\left( {e}_{11} - {e}_{22}\right) }^{2} + 4{e}_{12}^{2}}}\right\rbrack .
$$

11. 已知物体内某点的应变分量在原坐标系中的表示为 ${e}_{11} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}$ ,${e}_{22} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{33} = - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{12} = {0.025} \times {10}^{-3},{e}_{23} = 0,{e}_{31} = - {0.025} \times$​${10}^{-3}$ . 试求当坐标轴绕 ${x}_{2}$ 轴右旋 ${60}^{ \circ }$ 时,以新坐标系 ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 表示时的应变张量.

答案: 其矩阵形式为

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} {e}_{11}^{\prime } & {e}_{21}^{\prime } & {e}_{31}^{\prime } \\ {e}_{12}^{\prime } & {e}_{22}^{\prime } & {e}_{32}^{\prime } \\ {e}_{13}^{\prime } & {e}_{23}^{\prime } & {e}_{33}^{\prime } \end{array}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \frac{1}{2} & 0 & \frac{-\sqrt{3}}{2} \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \\ \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} & 0 & \frac{1}{2} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} {0.1} \times {10}^{-3} & {0.025} \times {10}^{-3} & - {0.025} \times {10}^{-3} \\ {0.025} \times {10}^{-3} & {0.1} \times {10}^{-3} & 0 \\ - {0.025} \times {10}^{-3} & 0 & - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \frac{1}{2} & 0 & \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \\ \frac{-\sqrt{3}}{2} & 0 & \frac{1}{2} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack
$$

12. 已知物体内某点的应变状态以直角坐标系表示时的应变分量为 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}$ 、 ${e}_{33}\text{、}{e}_{12}\text{、}{e}_{23}\text{、}{e}_{31}$ ,试求以柱坐标系表示时的应变分量.

答案: ${e}_{r} = {e}_{11}{\cos }^{2}\theta + {e}_{22}{\sin }^{2}\theta + 2{e}_{12}\sin \theta \cos \theta$ ,

${e}_{\theta } = {e}_{11}{\sin }^{2}\theta + {e}_{22}{\cos }^{2}\theta - 2{e}_{12}\sin \theta \cos \theta ,{e}_{z} = {e}_{33},$

${e}_{r\theta } = \left( {{e}_{22} - {e}_{11}}\right) \sin \theta \cos \theta + {e}_{12}\left( {{\cos }^{2}\theta - {\sin }^{2}\theta }\right) ,\;{e}_{\theta z} = {e}_{23}\cos \theta - {e}_{31}\sin \theta ,$

$$
{e}_{zr} = {e}_{23}\sin \theta + {e}_{31}\cos \theta .
$$

13. 设弹性体中任意点的位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = A{x}_{1} + B{x}_{2}^{2} - C{x}_{2}{x}_{3},{u}_{2} = A{x}_{1} + B{x}_{2} +$ $C{x}_{1}{x}_{3},{u}_{3} = A{x}_{1} + B{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + C{x}_{3}$ . 试求此弹性体内的体积应变.

答案: $\theta = A + B + C$ .

14. 试确定下列各应变状态是否存在:

(1) ${e}_{11} = k\left( {{x}_{1}^{2} + {x}_{2}^{2}}\right) ,{e}_{22} = k{x}_{2}^{2}{x}_{3},{e}_{33} = 0,{e}_{12} = k{x}_{1}{x}_{2}{x}_{3},{e}_{23} = 0,{e}_{31} = 0$ ;

(2) ${e}_{11} = k\left( {{x}_{1}^{2} + {x}_{2}^{2}}\right) ,{e}_{22} = k{x}_{2}^{2},{e}_{33} = 0,{e}_{12} = k{x}_{1}{x}_{2},{e}_{23} = 0,{e}_{31} = 0$ ;

(3) ${e}_{11} = \alpha {x}_{1}{x}_{2}^{2},{e}_{22} = \alpha {x}_{1}^{2}{x}_{2},{e}_{33} = a{x}_{1}{x}_{2},{e}_{12} = 0,{e}_{23} = a{x}_{1}^{2} + b{x}_{2},{e}_{31} = a{x}_{1}^{2} +$ $b{x}_{2}^{4}$ . 式中, $k\text{、}a\text{、}b$ 均为常数.

答案: (1) 不存在; (2) 存在; (3) 不存在.

15. 已知应变分量为 ${e}_{11} = \frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi /\partial {x}_{2}^{2} - \mu {\partial }^{2}\varphi /\partial {x}_{1}^{2}}{E},{e}_{22} = \frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi /\partial {x}_{1}^{2} - \mu {\partial }^{2}\varphi /\partial {x}_{2}^{2}}{E}$ ,

${e}_{12} = - \left( {1 + \mu }\right) \frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi /\partial {x}_{1}\partial {x}_{2}}{E},{e}_{33} = {e}_{23} = {e}_{31} = 0$ . 试确定函数 $\left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2}}\right)$ 应满足的方程式.

答案: ${\partial }^{4}\varphi /\partial {x}_{1}^{4} + 2{\partial }^{4}\varphi /\partial {x}_{1}^{2}\partial {x}_{2}^{2} + {\partial }^{4}\varphi /\partial {x}_{2}^{4} = 0$ .

16. 已知位移分量为 ${u}_{1} = \frac{{x}_{3}^{2} + \mu \left( {{x}_{1}^{2} - {x}_{2}^{2}}\right) }{2\alpha },{u}_{2} = \frac{\mu {x}_{1}{x}_{2}}{\alpha },{u}_{3} = - \frac{{x}_{1}{x}_{3}}{\alpha }$ ,式中, $\alpha \text{、}\mu$ 为常数. 试求应变分量, 并指出它们能否满足应变协调方程.

答案: ${e}_{11} = \frac{\mu {x}_{1}}{\alpha },{e}_{22} = \frac{\mu {x}_{1}}{\alpha },{e}_{33} = - \frac{{x}_{1}}{\alpha },{e}_{12} = {e}_{23} = {e}_{31} = 0$ ; 满足应变协调方程.

## 第 4 章

## 应力与应变的关系

对弹性物体在外载作用下产生的应力与应变的问题, 第 2 、第 3 章中已作了较为详细的讨论. 但没有涉及二者之间的关系问题. 事实上, 对于弹性介质来说, 应力与应变存在着相互依赖的关系. 因此, 有必要对物体受力与变形间的关系作进一步的讨论, 以便从物体的形状改变确定物体内部各点的应力数值, 反过来, 也可由物体的受力状态确定物体的形变状态.

本章主要叙述以应力表示应变的广义胡克定律和以应变表示应力的广义胡克定律. 这是弹性理论中十分重要的定律, 也是解决具体的弹性力学问题时最常用的定律. 此外, 还将叙述应变位能和弹性常数间的关系等重要内容.

## 4. 1 广义胡克定律

由前面的讨论知道, 物体内一点的应力状态由 6 个应力分量确定, 而同一点附近的应变状态由 6 个应变分量确定. 对小变形物体而言, 应力与应变之间存在线性关系. 即“在弹性体中的任一点, 6 个应力分量中的每个应力都是 6 个应变分量的线性函数, 反之亦然. ”这个规律称为广义胡克定律.

按此定律, 弹性体内任一点的应力与应变的关系式, 在没有初始应力和小变形的情况下,一般可写为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1133}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{1112} + {c}_{1121}}\right) {e}_{12} + \left( {{c}_{1123} + {c}_{1132}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{1113} + {c}_{1131}}\right) {e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{2211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2233}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{2212} + {c}_{2221}}\right) {e}_{12} + \left( {{c}_{2223} + {c}_{2232}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{2213} + {c}_{2231}}\right) {e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {c}_{3311}{e}_{11} + {c}_{3322}{e}_{22} + {c}_{3333}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{3312} + {c}_{3321}}\right) {e}_{12} + \left( {{c}_{3323} + {c}_{3332}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{3313} + {c}_{3331}}\right) {e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {c}_{1211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1233}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{1212} + {c}_{1221}}\right) {e}_{12} + \left( {{c}_{1223} + {c}_{1232}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{1213} + {c}_{1231}}\right) {e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {c}_{2311}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2322}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2333}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{2312} + {c}_{2321}}\right) {e}_{12} + \left( {{c}_{2323} + {c}_{2332}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{2313} + {c}_{2331}}\right) {e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = {c}_{3111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{3122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{3133}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{3112} + {c}_{3121}}\right) {e}_{12} + \left( {{c}_{3123} + {c}_{3132}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{3113} + {c}_{3131}}\right) {e}_{31} \tag{4.1}
$$

该式可以写成如下的哑指标形式:

$$
{\sigma }_{ji} = {c}_{jikl}{e}_{kl} \tag{4.2}
$$

式 (4.1) 或式 (4.2) 就是一般情况下的广义胡克定律. 式中 ${c}_{jikl}$ 均为比例常数,它们的数值由材料的弹性性质决定. 可以证明,对于一个保守系统,有 ${c}_{jikl} = {c}_{klji},{c}_{jikl} =$ ${c}_{jilk}$ ,即 ${c}_{1122} = {c}_{2211},{c}_{1112} = {c}_{1121},{c}_{2213} = {c}_{2231} = {c}_{3122}$ 等 (证明见本章 4.5 节). 按此结论, 式(4.1)变为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1133}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{1112}{e}_{12} + 2{c}_{1123}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{1131}{e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{2211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2233}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{2212}{e}_{12} + 2{c}_{2223}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{2231}{e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {c}_{3311}{e}_{11} + {c}_{3322}{e}_{22} + {c}_{3333}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{3312}{e}_{12} + 2{c}_{3323}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{3331}{e}_{31} \tag{4. 3}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {c}_{1211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1233}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12} + 2{c}_{1223}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{1231}{e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {c}_{2311}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2322}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2333}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{2312}{e}_{12} + 2{c}_{2323}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{2331}{e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = {c}_{3111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{3122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{3133}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{3112}{e}_{12} + 2{c}_{3123}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{3131}{e}_{31}
$$

将其写为矩阵形式, 则为(4. 4)

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_71_422_837_877_343_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_71_422_837_877_343_0-20241011170328-ancpkm1.jpg)

式中, 6 个对角元素为独立的弹性常数, 其余 30 个非对角线元素两两相等或成倍数关系. 即对保守系统来说, 独立的弹性常数为 21 个. 对于不同的弹性物质, 其独立的弹性常数不同. 最简单的情况是各向同性物质, 独立的弹性常数只有两个. 由此可见, 对各向异性物质的讨论, 远比各向同性物质复杂得多, 而各向同性的假定往往是地球内部介质很好的近似. 因此, 本书着重讨论各向同性体内应力与应变的关系.

## 4.2 以应变表示应力的广义胡克定律

对各向同性物质来说, 在小变形的情况下, 应力与应变的线性关系在各个方向上应该不变, 也即当坐标轴旋转至任意方向时, 应力与应变的关系或比例常数应该不变. 因此, 可以利用坐标轴的旋转推导各向同性体内以应变表示应力的广义胡克定律.

为清楚方便起见,首先将坐标轴做 ${180}^{ \circ }$ 的旋转,如果转动的是 ${x}_{3}$ 轴,即 ${x}_{3}$ 轴的方向改为相反的方向,则 ${x}_{3}$ 和 ${u}_{3}$ 的正、负号改为相反的符号,因此

$$
{c}_{23} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}/\partial {x}_{2} + \partial {u}_{2}/\partial {x}_{3}}{2}
$$

与

$$
{c}_{31} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}/\partial {x}_{3} + \partial {u}_{3}/\partial {x}_{1}}{2}
$$

也将改变其正、负号. 由于 ${x}_{3}$ 轴转为相反方向后,式 (4.3) 中的 ${\sigma }_{11}\text{、}{\sigma }_{22}\text{、}{\sigma }_{33}$ (拉应力为正,压应力为负)、 ${\sigma }_{12}$ 并不受影响,与其对应的各式右端的前四项也不变,而后两项保持其数值改变正、负号. 欲使 ${\sigma }_{11}\text{、}{\sigma }_{22}\text{、}{\sigma }_{33}\text{、}{\sigma }_{12}$ 不因 ${x}_{3}$ 轴改为相反方向而改变其正、负号或出现量值突变,只有 ${c}_{1123} = {c}_{1131} = {c}_{2223} = {c}_{2231} = {c}_{3323} = {c}_{3331} = {c}_{1223} = {c}_{1231} = 0$ 时, 方程式 (4.3) 中的前四式才能成立.

对于方程式 (4.3) 的后两式,当 ${x}_{3}$ 轴转为相反方向后, ${\sigma }_{23}$ 与 ${\sigma }_{31}$ 保持原数值但改变其正、负号, 而等式右端的前四项并不改变正、负号. 因此, 欲使应力与应变的关系在各个方向上保持不变, 即当应力改变正、负号时应变也随之改变正、 负号,则必须是 ${c}_{2311} = {c}_{2322} = {c}_{2333} = {c}_{2312} = {c}_{3111} = {c}_{3122} = {c}_{3133} = {c}_{3112} = 0$ . 此时, 式(4.3)成为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1133}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{1112}{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{2211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2233}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{2212}{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {c}_{3311}{e}_{11} + {c}_{3322}{e}_{22} + {c}_{3333}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{3312}{e}_{12} \tag{4.5}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {c}_{1211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1233}{e}_{33} + 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = 2{c}_{2323}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{2331}{e}_{31}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = 2{c}_{3123}{e}_{23} + 2{c}_{3131}{e}_{31}
$$

在此基础上,若将 ${x}_{2}$ 轴转动 ${180}^{ \circ }$ 而其他两轴不变, ${x}_{2}$ 与 ${u}_{2}$ 改为相反的符号,因此

$$
{c}_{12} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}/\partial {x}_{1} + \partial {u}_{1}/\partial {x}_{2}}{2}
$$

与

$$
{c}_{23} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}/\partial {x}_{2} + \partial {u}_{2}/\partial {x}_{3}}{2}
$$

改变其正、负号. 而式 (4.5) 左端除 ${\sigma }_{12}$ 与 ${\sigma }_{23}$ 改变正、负号外,其余四项均不受其影响. 按照相同的理由,必有 ${c}_{1112} = {c}_{2212} = {c}_{3312} = {c}_{1211} = {c}_{1222} = {c}_{1233} = {c}_{2331} = {c}_{3123} = 0$ . 此时式(4.5)变为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1133}{e}_{33}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{2211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2233}{e}_{33}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {c}_{3311}{e}_{11} + {c}_{3322}{e}_{22} + {c}_{3333}{e}_{33} \tag{4. 6}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = 2{c}_{2323}{e}_{23}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = 2{c}_{3131}{e}_{31}
$$

同样,若再将 ${x}_{1}$ 轴旋转 ${180}^{ \circ }$ 而 ${x}_{2}\text{、}{x}_{3}$ 轴不变,则因为式 (4.6) 中应变分量只有 ${e}_{12}$ 与 ${e}_{31}$ 改变正、负号,而等式左端只有与 ${e}_{12}\text{、}{e}_{31}$ 相对应的 ${\sigma }_{12}\text{、}{\sigma }_{31}$ 改变正、负号,因此, 式(4.6)保持不变.

由式 (4.6) 可以看出,弹性常数还有 12 个,若考虑到 ${c}_{jikl} = {c}_{klji}$ ,则式中的弹性常数又减少 3 个, 故式 (4.6) 中实际上只有 9 个独立的弹性常数. 通过上述讨论可知, 式 (4.6) 是将各坐标轴转为相反方向且认为其弹性关系不变而得到的方程式. 因此, 通常将其称为正交各向异性体内的广义胡克定律.

按照相同的方法,将各坐标轴做 ${90}^{ \circ }$ 的转动. 比如, ${x}_{2}$ 轴与 ${x}_{3}$ 轴互换,则方程式 (4.6) 的第一式中, ${\sigma }_{11}$ 的正、负号不变,而等式右端的 ${e}_{22}$ 与 ${e}_{33}$ 彼此互换位置. 此时,只有 ${c}_{1122} = {c}_{1133}$ 时,该式两端才能相等. 同时,由于 ${\sigma }_{12}$ 成为 ${\sigma }_{13}\left( { = {\sigma }_{31}}\right) ,{e}_{12}$ 成为 ${e}_{13}\left( { = {e}_{31}}\right)$ ,即 ${e}_{31}$ 和 ${\sigma }_{31}$ 分别为 ${e}_{21}$ 和 ${\sigma }_{21}$ ,这相当于方程 (4.6) 的第四与第六式除弹性系数 ${c}_{1212}\text{、}{c}_{3131}$ 外互换位置. 这只有在 ${c}_{1212} = {c}_{3131}$ 时,才能做此置换. 同样,再将 ${x}_{3}$ 与 ${x}_{1},{x}_{1}$ 与 ${x}_{2}$ 轴互换,可得 ${c}_{1122} = {c}_{1133} = {c}_{2211} = {c}_{3311} = {c}_{2233} = {c}_{3322},{c}_{1212} = {c}_{2323} = {c}_{3131}$ . 于是式 (4.6) 成为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{2222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{33}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {c}_{3333}{e}_{33} + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) \tag{4.7}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{23}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{31}
$$

又因为在 ${x}_{2}$ 与 ${x}_{3}$ 轴互换时, ${\sigma }_{22}$ 与 ${\sigma }_{33}$ 互换, ${e}_{22}$ 与 ${e}_{33}$ 互换,由式 (4.7) 中的二、三式得 ${c}_{2222} = {c}_{3333}$ . 同样,在 ${x}_{1}$ 与 ${x}_{2}$ 轴互换时, ${\sigma }_{11}$ 与 ${\sigma }_{22}$ 互换, ${e}_{11}$ 与 ${e}_{22}$ 互换,由式 (4.7) 的前两式得 ${c}_{1111} = {c}_{2222}$ . 将 ${c}_{1111} = {c}_{2222} = {c}_{3333}$ 代入式 (4.7),便得

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{33}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{33} + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) \tag{4. 8}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{23}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{31}
$$

由于式 (4.8) 是将各坐标轴做 ${90}^{ \circ }$ 转动,认为其弹性关系不变而得到的方程式,因此通常称为正交各向同性体内的广义胡克定律.

对各向同性物质, 坐标轴转动任意角度后, 弹性关系不变, 即应有

$$
{\sigma }_{11}^{\prime } = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11}^{\prime } + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{22}^{\prime } + {e}_{33}^{\prime }}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22}^{\prime } = {c}_{1111}{e}_{22}^{\prime } + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{11}^{\prime } + {e}_{33}^{\prime }}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33}^{\prime } = {c}_{1111}{e}_{33}^{\prime } + {c}_{1122}\left( {{e}_{11}^{\prime } + {e}_{22}^{\prime }}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12}^{\prime } = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12}^{\prime }
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23}^{\prime } = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{23}^{\prime }
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31}^{\prime } = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{31}^{\prime } \tag{4.9}
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_74_946_253_533_408_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_74_946_253_533_408_0-20241011170328-g8xvcij.jpg)

图 4-1

现在,取 ${x}_{3}^{\prime }$ 轴与 ${x}_{3}$ 轴重合, ${x}_{1}^{\prime }$ 与 ${x}_{1}$ 轴间的夹角为 $\varphi$ (图 4-1). 很明显, ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 系的各轴对 ${x}_{i}$ 系各轴的方向余弦如表 4-1 所示. 将表 4-1 中所列方向余弦代入应力张量及应变张量的坐标变换公式 (2.55) 与式 (3.48), 得

$$
{\sigma }_{12}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{21}{\sigma }_{11} + {\alpha }_{11}{\alpha }_{22}{\sigma }_{12} + {\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{21}{\sigma }_{21} + {\alpha }_{12}{\alpha }_{22}{\sigma }_{22}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\sin {2\varphi }\left( {{\sigma }_{22} - {\sigma }_{11}}\right) + \cos {2\varphi } \cdot {\sigma }_{12}
$$

$$
{e}_{12}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2}\sin {2\varphi }\left( {{e}_{22} - {e}_{11}}\right) + \cos {2\varphi } \cdot {e}_{12} \tag{4.10}
$$

表 4-1

<div>
<table><thead><tr><th>变量</th><th>$ {x}_{1} $</th><th>$ {x}_{2} $</th><th>$ {x}_{3} $</th></tr></thead><tr><td>$ {x}_{1}^{\prime } $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{11}\left( {\cos \varphi }\right) $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{12}\left( {\sin \varphi }\right) $</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>$ {x}_{2}^{\prime } $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{21}\left( {-\sin \varphi }\right) $</td><td>$ {\alpha }_{22}\left( {\cos \varphi }\right) $</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>$ {x}_{3}^{\prime } $</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr></table>
</div>

将式 (4.10) 代入到式 (4.9) 中的第四式, 得

$$
\left\lbrack {\frac{1}{2}\sin {2\varphi }\left( {{\sigma }_{22} - {\sigma }_{11}}\right) + \cos {2\varphi } \cdot {\sigma }_{12}}\right\rbrack = 2{c}_{1212}\left\lbrack {\frac{1}{2}\sin {2\varphi }\left( {{e}_{22} - {e}_{11}}\right) + \cos {2\varphi } \cdot {e}_{12}}\right\rbrack \tag{4.11}
$$

因为 ${\sigma }_{12} = 2{c}_{1212}{e}_{12}$ ,故式 (4.11) 可变为

$$
{\sigma }_{22} - {\sigma }_{11} = 2{c}_{1212}\left( {{e}_{22} - {e}_{11}}\right) \tag{4.12}
$$

再将式 (4.8) 中的第一、第二式代入式 (4.12), 得

$$
\left( {{c}_{1111} - {c}_{1122}}\right) \left( {{e}_{22} - {e}_{11}}\right) = 2{e}_{1212}\left( {{e}_{22} - {e}_{11}}\right)
$$

从而有

$$
{c}_{1111} - {c}_{1122} = 2{c}_{1212} \tag{4. 13}
$$

由此可见, 对各向同性物质来说, 式 (4.8) 中 3 个弹性常数受式 (4.13) 的制约, 故独立的弹性常数只有两个. 若取 ${c}_{1122}$ 和 ${c}_{1212}$ 是独立的,则

$$
{c}_{1111} = {c}_{1122} + 2{c}_{1212} \tag{\left {4,{14}}\right}
$$

若令 ${c}_{1122} = \lambda ,{c}_{1212} = \mu$ ,则式 (4.15) 成为

$$
{c}_{1111} = \lambda + {2\mu } \tag{4. 15}
$$

将其代入式 (4.8), 则得

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{33} \tag{4. 16}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {2\mu }{e}_{23}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{31} = {2\mu }{e}_{31}
$$

式中, $\theta = {e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}$ 为体积应变. 若将式 (4.16) 用哑指标表示,则为

$$
{\sigma }_{ji} = {\lambda \theta }{\delta }_{ji} + {2\mu }{e}_{ji} \tag{4.17}
$$

式(4.16)或式(4.17)即为各向同性体内以应变表示应力的广义胡克定律.

例 4-1 用应力解除法计算地应力.

解 在测量地应力时, 通常采用如下方法, 即在测量点钻一竖直小孔, 将等角应变化或直角应变化水平地放入孔内, 记下初始读数. 然后在离孔壁较远处 (一般是圆孔直径的 3-5 倍) 开一同心圆槽, 使中间的圆柱与周围岩体隔离, 这时中间圆柱从原来受力状态卸载,应变花上出现新的读数. 通过两次的读数便可断定 3 个水平方向上的线应变 (或正应变). 设等角应变化的测值为 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ ,根据例 3-1 的讨论可知, 平面应变分量为

$$
{e}_{11} = {e}_{0}
$$

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{{e}_{60} - {e}_{120}}{\sqrt{3}}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = \frac{2\left( {{e}_{60} + {e}_{120}}\right) - {e}_{0}}{3}
$$

欲求应力分量, 只需将此应变分量代入式 (4.16) 便得

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{11} = 2\left\lbrack {\frac{\lambda \left( {{e}_{0} + {e}_{60} + {e}_{120}}\right) }{3} + \mu {e}_{0}}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{22} = \frac{2\left\lbrack {\left( {\lambda + {2\mu }}\right) \left( {{e}_{60} + {e}_{120}}\right) + \left( {\lambda - \mu }\right) {e}_{0}}\right\rbrack }{3}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{33} = \frac{{2\lambda }\left( {{e}_{0} + {e}_{60} + {e}_{120}}\right) }{3}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12} = \frac{2\sqrt{3}\mu \left( {{e}_{60} - {e}_{120}}\right) }{3}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0
$$

式中, $\lambda \text{、}\mu$ 为所求点的拉梅常数.

值得注意的是, 在上述计算过程中, 无形地假定了卸载前后圆柱体在竖直方向上没有相对伸长或相对缩短, 这相当于竖直方向上的应变完全被限制住. 限制应变的外力会使物体内部的应力发生改变. 因此在竖直方向上虽然没有应变, 但可有应力的作用. 如果在竖直方向上不加如上假定, 则不能按此计算.

## 4.3 以应力表示应变的广义胡克定律

## 4.3.1 理论弹性常数与实测常数间的关系

以简单拉伸模型为例,此时 ${\sigma }_{11} \neq 0,{\sigma }_{22} = {\sigma }_{33} = {\sigma }_{12} = {\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0$ (图 4-2). 代入以应变表达应力的广义胡克定律有

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
0 = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{22} \tag{4. 18}
$$

$$
0 = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{33}
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_76_996_759_493_428_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_76_996_759_493_428_0-20241011170328-oacmfjq.jpg)

图 4-2

将三式相加, 得

$$
\left( {{3\lambda } + {2\mu }}\right) \theta = {\sigma }_{11} \tag{4.19}
$$

再将其代入式(4.18)第一式, 得

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \frac{\mu \left( {{3\lambda } + {2\mu }}\right) }{\lambda + \mu }{e}_{11} \tag{4.20}
$$

将其与实验结果式 (1.25) 进行比较, 有

$$
E = \frac{\mu \left( {{3\lambda } + {2\mu }}\right) }{\lambda + \mu } \tag{4. 21}
$$

其次, 将式 (4.19) 代入式 (4.18) 中的第二或第三式, 得

$$
\frac{\lambda }{{3\lambda } + {2\mu }}{\sigma }_{11} + {2\mu }{e}_{22}\text{ (或 }{e}_{33}\text{ ) } = 0
$$

整理得

$$
- \frac{{e}_{22}}{{e}_{11}} = - \frac{{e}_{33}}{{e}_{11}} = \frac{\lambda }{2\left( {\lambda + \mu }\right) } \tag{4.22}
$$

将其与实验结果式 (1.26) 进行比较, 得

$$
\nu = \frac{\lambda }{2\left( {\lambda + \mu }\right) } \tag{4.23}
$$

由式(4.21)与式(4.23)联立求解, 得

$$
\lambda = \frac{\nu E}{\left( {1 + \nu }\right) \left( {1 - {2\nu }}\right) }
$$

$$
\mu = \frac{E}{2\left( {1 + \nu }\right) } \tag{4.24}
$$

式(4.24) 即为理论常数与实测常数的关系.

## 4. 3. 2 体积应变定律

由于体积应变只与应变张量的对角元素 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{22}\text{、}{e}_{33}$ 有关,故由广义胡克定律可有

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{33} \tag{4.25}
$$

将三式相加, 得

$$
{\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33} = \left( {{3\lambda } + {2\mu }}\right) \theta
$$

令 $\Theta = {\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33}$ 并代入 $\lambda \text{、}\mu$ 得

$$
\theta = \frac{1 - {2\nu }}{E} \tag{4.26}
$$

式(4.26)称为体积应变定律.

## 4. 3.3 以应力表示应变的广义胡克定律

将体积应变定律代入广义胡克定律的第一式

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = {\lambda \theta } + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

得

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \frac{1 - {2\nu }}{E}\Theta + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

再将 $\lambda \text{、}\mu$ 代入并整理得

$$
{e}_{11} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{11}
$$

同理,将体积应变定律及 $\lambda \text{、}\mu$ 代入广义胡克定律中的后五式,可得下式中的后五式, 即

$$
{e}_{11} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{11}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{22}
$$

$$
{e}_{33} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{33}
$$

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{12}
$$

$$
{e}_{23} = \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{23}
$$

$$
{e}_{31} = \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{31} \tag{4.27}
$$

写成哑指标形式则为

$$
{e}_{ij} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta {\delta }_{ij} + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{ij} \tag{4. 28}
$$

式(4.27) 或式(4.28) 称为以应力表示应变的广义胡克定律.

例 4-2 弹性体中某一点在 ${x}_{1}\text{、}{x}_{2}$ 方向上的正应力为 ${\sigma }_{11} = 1\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}\text{、}{\sigma }_{22} =$ $2\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}$ ,沿 ${x}_{3}$ 方向上的应变完全被限制住. 试求 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{12}$ 和 ${\sigma }_{33}(E = {2.1} \times {10}^{5}\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}$ , $\nu = {0.3}$ ).

解 此题有三种解法. 一是利用以应力表示应变的广义胡克定律, 列出

$$
{e}_{11} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{11}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{22}
$$

$$
0 = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{33}
$$

式中, $\nu \text{、}E\text{、}{\sigma }_{11}\text{、}{\sigma }_{22}$ 均为已知量 $\Theta = {\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33}$ . 由此 3 个方程可解出当中的 3 个未知数 ${e}_{11}\text{、}{e}_{12}$ 和 ${\sigma }_{33}$ . 即

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = \frac{\nu \left( {1 - \nu }\right) \left( {{\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{33}}\right) }{\left( {1 + \nu }\right) \left( {1 - {2\nu }}\right) + 2{\nu }^{2}} = {0.894}\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}
$$

$$
{e}_{11} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\left( {{\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33}}\right) + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{11} = {6.27} \times {10}^{-7}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = - \frac{\nu }{E}\left( {{\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33}}\right) + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{22} = {6.82} \times {10}^{-6}
$$

此题的第二种解法是应用以应变表示应力的广义胡克定律, 列如下方程:

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right)
$$

式中, $\lambda \text{、}\mu$ 可由 $E\text{、}\nu$ 求得,视为已知,故由此 3 个方程也可求出 3 个未知量 ${\sigma }_{33}\text{、}{e}_{11}$ 、 ${e}_{22}$ . 其结果与前一种解法一致.

此题的第三种解法是两个广义胡克定律同时使用, 列出如下方程:

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
0 = - \frac{\nu }{E}\Theta + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{33}
$$

该方程中也只有 3 个未知数, 故可求解, 其结果与前面相同. 由此可见, 以应变表示应力的广义胡克定律与以应力表示应变的广义胡克定律实际上是等同的, 只是根据使用的方便选定.

## 4.4 应变势能

如前所述, 物体在外力作用下将产生变形. 对完全弹性体来说, 当外载撤除后, 物体将恢复到受力前的状态. 从这点出发, 可以把外力作用使物体发生形变看成是外力对物体做功, 而外力撤除物体恢复原来形状过程看成是物体的释能过程. 因此, 对完全弹性物体, 当其发生变形后将在弹性体内储存一定的能量. 这个能量就是应变势能.

由于物体所受的力可分为体力 ${\int }_{V}\rho {f}_{i}\mathrm{\;d}V$ 与面力 ${\oint }_{S}{\sigma }_{ni}\mathrm{\;d}S$ ,因此外力对物体做功也应是体力做功与面力做功之和,当设位移函数为 $\delta {u}_{i}$ 时,体力对物体所做的功为

$$
{A}_{P} = {\int }_{V}\rho \left( {{f}_{i}\delta {u}_{i}}\right) \mathrm{d}V \tag{4.29}
$$

面力做功为

$$
{A}_{S} = {\oint }_{S}{\sigma }_{ni}\delta {u}_{i}\mathrm{\;d}S \tag{4.30}
$$

考虑到 ${\sigma }_{ni} = {\sigma }_{ji}{n}_{j}$ ,式 (4.30) 可变为

$$
{A}_{S} = {\oint }_{S}{\sigma }_{ji}{n}_{j}\delta {u}_{i}\mathrm{\;d}S \tag{4. 31}
$$

利用高斯定理

$$
{\oint }_{S}{A}_{i}{n}_{i}\mathrm{\;d}S = {\int }_{V}\frac{\partial {A}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{i}}\mathrm{\;d}V
$$

将式 (4.31) 化为体积积分的形式, 即

$$
{A}_{S} = {\int }_{V}\frac{\partial }{\partial {x}_{j}}\left( {{\sigma }_{ji}\delta {u}_{i}}\right) \mathrm{d}V = {\int }_{V}\left( {\frac{\partial {\sigma }_{ji}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\delta {u}_{i} + {\sigma }_{ji}\frac{\partial \delta {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}}\right) \mathrm{d}V \tag{4.32}
$$

因此, 总功为

$$
A = {A}_{P} + {A}_{S} = {\int }_{V}\left\lbrack {\left( {\rho {f}_{i} + \frac{\partial {\sigma }_{ji}}{\partial {x}_{j}}}\right) \delta {u}_{i} + {\sigma }_{ji}\delta \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}}\right\rbrack \mathrm{d}V \tag{4. 33}
$$

由前面所讲的平衡微分方程

$$
\frac{\partial {\sigma }_{ji}}{\partial {x}_{j}} + \rho {f}_{i} = 0
$$

当物体处于平衡状态时,总功 $A$ 为

$$
A = {\int }_{V}{\sigma }_{ji}\delta \left( \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\right) \mathrm{d}V \tag{4.34}
$$

此式还可写成

$$
A = {\int }_{V}\frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {{\sigma }_{ji}\delta \left( \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\right) + {\sigma }_{ji}\delta \left( \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\right) }\right\rbrack \mathrm{d}V
$$

$$
= {\int }_{V}\frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {{\sigma }_{ji}\delta \left( \frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}}\right) + {\sigma }_{ij}\delta \left( \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}\right) }\right\rbrack \mathrm{d}V
$$

(利用哑指标规则 3)

$$
= {\int }_{V}\frac{1}{2}{\sigma }_{ji}\delta \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{i}}{\partial {x}_{j}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}}}\right) \mathrm{d}V\;\left( {{\sigma }_{ji} = {\sigma }_{ij}}\right)
$$

$$
= {\int }_{V}{\sigma }_{ji}\delta {e}_{ji}\mathrm{\;d}V \tag{4. 35}
$$

式 (4.35) 即为外力做功的表达式. 式中, ${e}_{ji}$ 为应变张量, ${\sigma }_{ji}$ 为应力张量. ${\sigma }_{ji}\delta {e}_{ji}$ 并称为体积元内单位体积上外力所做的功,若用符号 ${\delta A}$ 表示,则有

$$
{\delta A} = {\sigma }_{ji}\delta {e}_{ji} \tag{4. 36}
$$

如上所述, 对完全弹性体来说, 外力做功使物体的形状发生改变, 而外力撤除后物体恢复原来的形状, 在变形前后物体内部无耗散力做功, 或者说外力对物体做功完全转变为物体的形变能量. 因此有

$$
{\delta A} = {\delta W} = {\sigma }_{ji}\delta {e}_{ji} \tag{4. 37}
$$

式中, ${\delta W}$ 为体积元内单位体积的应变势能. 因为当 ${e}_{ji}$ 趋于零时, ${\delta W}$ 也趋于零,故应变势能是物体状态的单值函数. 于是式 (4.37) 可写为

$$
\frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{ji}} = {\sigma }_{ji} \tag{4. 38}
$$

既应变势能是物体状态的单值函数,所以应变势能 $W$ 也可用下列函数形式表示, 即

$$
W = f\left( {e}_{ji}\right) \tag{4. 39}
$$

对小变形而言,应变势能函数可作如下的泰勒展开

$$
W = {a}_{0} + {b}_{ji}{e}_{ji} + \frac{1}{2}{c}_{jikl}{e}_{ji}{e}_{kl} + o{\left( e\right) }^{2} \tag{4. 40}
$$

式中, ${a}_{0}\text{、}{b}_{ji}\text{、}{c}_{jikl}$ 为常数, $o{\left( e\right) }^{2}$ 为比 ${e}^{2}$ 更高级的无穷小量. 若将式 (4.40) 对 ${e}_{ji}$ 求导, 得

$$
\frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{ji}} = {b}_{ji} + {c}_{jikl}{e}_{kl} \tag{4.41}
$$

与式(4.38)对比, 有

$$
{\sigma }_{ji} = {b}_{ji} + {c}_{jikl}{e}_{kl} \tag{4.42}
$$

由于在无初始应力 (弹性力学基本假设之一) 情况下, 物体的应力分量为零时应变分量也为零. 所以有 ${b}_{ji} = 0$ ,因此,式 (4.42) 成为

$$
{\sigma }_{ji} = {c}_{jikl}{e}_{kl} \tag{4. 43}
$$

将其代入式 (4.40), 得

$$
W = \frac{1}{2}{\sigma }_{ji}{e}_{ji} \tag{4.44}
$$

此式即为应变势能公式. 将其展开, 则有

$$
W = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{\sigma }_{11}{e}_{11} + {\sigma }_{22}{e}_{22} + {\sigma }_{33}{e}_{33} + 2{\sigma }_{12}{e}_{12} + 2{\sigma }_{23}{e}_{23} + 2{\sigma }_{31}{e}_{31}}\right) \tag{4. 45}
$$

对各向同性物体来说, 应力张量与应变张量之间的关系由式 (4.17) 或式 (4.28) 决定. 因此, 在已知应变张量的情况下, 可将式 (4.17) 代入式 (4.44), 得

$$
W = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{\lambda \theta }{\delta }_{ji} + {2\mu }{e}_{ji}}\right) {e}_{ji} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{\lambda \theta }{e}_{ji}{\delta }_{ji} + {2\mu }{e}_{ji}{e}_{ji}}\right)
$$

因为 ${e}_{ji}{\delta }_{ji} = {e}_{11} + {e}_{23} + {e}_{33} = \theta$ ,所以有

$$
W = \frac{1}{2}\lambda {\theta }^{2} + \mu {e}_{ji}{e}_{ji} \tag{\left {4.46}\right}
$$

这便是以应变张量表示应变势能的公式. 同样, 如果将式 (4.28) 代入式 (4.44), 可得

$$
W = \frac{1}{2}{\sigma }_{ji}\left\lbrack {-\frac{\nu }{E}\Theta {\delta }_{ji} + \frac{1 + \nu }{E}{\sigma }_{ji}}\right\rbrack = \frac{1 + \nu }{2E}{\sigma }_{ji}{\sigma }_{ji} - \frac{\nu }{2E}\Theta {\sigma }_{ji}{\delta }_{ji}
$$

因为 ${\sigma }_{ji}{\delta }_{ji} = {\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33} = \Theta$ ,所以有

$$
W = \frac{1}{2E}\left\lbrack {\left( {1 + \nu }\right) {\sigma }_{ji}{\sigma }_{ji} - \nu {\Theta }^{2}}\right\rbrack \tag{4. 47}
$$

式(4.47) 是以应力张量表示应变势能的公式.

例 4-3 已知弹性体中任一点的位移分量为 ${u}_{1} \neq {10} \times {10}^{-3} + {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} +$​${0.05} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{3},{u}_{2} = 5 \times {10}^{-3} - {0.05} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1} + {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{2}{x}_{3},{u}_{3} = {10} \times {10}^{-3} -$​${0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2}{x}_{3}$ . 杨氏模量与泊松比分别为 $E = {2.1} \times {10}^{5}\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2},\nu = {0.3}$ ,试求点 $A\left( {1,1,1}\right)$ 的应变势能.

解 为求应变势能, 首先由位移分量求出应变分量. 利用应变张量表达式, 可得

$$
{e}_{11} = \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{1}} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{2} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{2}} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{3} = {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{33} = \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{3}} = - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} = - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{1}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{2}}}\right) = {0.025} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

$$
{e}_{23} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{2}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{2}}{\partial {x}_{3}}}\right) = 0
$$

$$
{e}_{31} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{1}}{\partial {x}_{3}} + \frac{\partial {u}_{3}}{\partial {x}_{1}}}\right) = - {0.025} \times {10}^{-3}
$$

再利用以应变张量表示应变势能的式 (4.46), 可得

$$
W = \frac{1}{2}\lambda {\theta }^{2} + \mu {e}_{ji}{e}_{ji} = \frac{1}{2}\lambda {\left( {e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}\right) }^{2} + \mu \left\lbrack {{e}_{11}^{2} + {e}_{22}^{2} + {e}_{33}^{2} + 2{e}_{12}^{2} + 2{e}_{23}^{2} + 2{e}_{31}^{2}}\right\rbrack
$$

式中, $\lambda \text{、}\mu$ 可由式 (4.24) 求得,即

$$
\lambda = \frac{\nu E}{\left( {1 + \nu }\right) \left( {1 - {2\nu }}\right) } = \frac{{0.3} \times {2.1} \times {10}^{5}}{\left( {1 + {0.3}}\right) \left( {1 - 2 \times {0.3}}\right) }
$$

$$
= {1.21} \times {10}^{5}\left( {\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
\mu = \frac{E}{2\left( {1 + \nu }\right) } = \frac{{2.1} \times {10}^{5}}{2\left( {1 + {0.3}}\right) }
$$

$$
= {0.81} \times {10}^{5}\left( {\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}}\right)
$$

将其代入前式并利用已求得的各应变分量, 有

$$
W = \left\{ {\frac{1}{2} \times {1.21} \times {10}^{5}{\left( {0.1} \times {10}^{-3} + {0.1} \times {10}^{-3} - {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}\right) }^{2}}\right.
$$

$$
+ {0.81} \times {10}^{5}\left\lbrack {{\left( {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}\right) }^{2} + {\left( {0.1} \times {10}^{-3}\right) }^{2} + {\left( -{0.1} \times {10}^{3}\right) }^{2}}\right.
$$

$$
\left. \left. {+2 \times {\left( {0.025} \times {10}^{-3}\right) }^{2} + 2 \times 0 + 2 \times {\left( -{0.025} \times {10}^{-3}\right) }^{2}}\right\rbrack \right\}
$$

$$
= {3.23} \times {10}^{-3}\left( {\mathrm{\;N}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= {3.23} \times {10}^{-6}\left( {\mathrm{\;J}/{\mathrm{{mm}}}^{3}}\right)
$$

由此可见, 一点的应变势能实际是指该点单位体积内所具有的应变能量.

## 4.5 应变势能与弹性常数的关系

对完全弹性体来说, 应变势能与应变张量及应力张量的微分关系由式 (4.38) 确定, 即

$$
\frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{ji}} = {\sigma }_{ji} \tag{4. 48}
$$

由于完全弹性体所构成的系统可以看成是保守系统, 因此由式 (4.48) 推导出的弹性常数间的关系, 自然对保守系统成立.

下面我们利用式 (4.48) 推导保守系统内的弹性常数间的关系. 取式 (4.48) 中的 $i = j = 1$ 并考虑到式(4.1),得

$$
\frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{11}} = {\sigma }_{11} = {c}_{1111}{e}_{11} + {c}_{1122}{e}_{22} + {c}_{1133}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{1112} + {c}_{1121}}\right) {e}_{12}
$$

$$
+ \left( {{c}_{1123} + {c}_{1132}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{1113} + {c}_{1131}}\right) {e}_{31} \tag{4. 49}
$$

同样,若取 $i = j = 2$ ,则

$$
\frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{22}} = {\sigma }_{22} = {c}_{2211}{e}_{11} + {c}_{2222}{e}_{22} + {c}_{2233}{e}_{33} + \left( {{c}_{2212} + {c}_{2221}}\right) {e}_{12}
$$

$$
+ \left( {{c}_{2223} + {c}_{2232}}\right) {e}_{23} + \left( {{c}_{2213} + {c}_{2231}}\right) {e}_{31} \tag{4. 50}
$$

因为应变势能是物体状态的单值函数, 因此有

$$
\frac{{\partial }^{2}W}{\partial {e}_{11}\partial {e}_{22}} = \frac{{\partial }^{2}W}{\partial {e}_{22}\partial {e}_{11}} \tag{4. 51}
$$

将式 (4.49) 及式 (4.50) 代入式 (4.51), 得

$$
\frac{\partial }{\partial {e}_{22}}\left( \frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{11}}\right) = {c}_{1122} \tag{4. 52}
$$

$$
\frac{\partial }{\partial {e}_{11}}\left( \frac{\partial W}{\partial {e}_{22}}\right) = {c}_{2211}
$$

由此得

$$
{c}_{1122} = {c}_{2211} \tag{4. 53}
$$

同理, 可以证明式 (4.1) 中其他系数间也存在两两相等或简单的 2 倍关系. 例如,

${c}_{2233} = {c}_{3322},{c}_{1133} = {c}_{3311},{c}_{1113} = {c}_{1131},{c}_{1113} + {c}_{1131} = 2{c}_{3111}$ ,等等. 写成数学表示式则为

$$
{c}_{jikl} = {c}_{jilk}
$$

$$
{c}_{jikl} = {c}_{klji} \tag{4. 54}
$$

因此, 对一个保守系统来说, 弹性常数的数目为式 (4.4) 中 6 个对角元素与 15 个独立的非对角元素之和, 共计 21 个. 它是极端各向异性物质内的弹性常数. 对于不同的物质, 独立的弹性常数不同, 现将各晶系的弹性常数列于表 4-2 中, 作为参考.

表 4-2 各晶系的弹性常数

<div>
<table><thead><tr><th>三斜晶系</th><th>单斜晶系</th><th>斜方晶系</th><th>正方晶系</th><th>六角晶系</th><th>立方晶系</th><th>各向同性体</th></tr></thead><tr><td>21</td><td>13</td><td>9</td><td>7</td><td>5</td><td>3</td><td>2</td></tr></table>
</div>

## 讨 论

## 一、二维测量与三维改变量之间的关系

以等角应变花测量方法为例,设与 ${x}_{1}$ 轴平行、与 ${x}_{1}$ 轴成 ${60}^{ \circ }$ 角、与 ${x}_{1}$ 轴成 ${120}^{ \circ }$ 角的 3 个方向上的正应变 (线应变) 值分别为 ${e}_{0}\text{、}{e}_{60}\text{、}{e}_{120}$ ,应变张量为 ${e}_{ji}(j, i =$ $1,2,3)$ ,则平面应变分量由例 3-1 可知为

$$
{e}_{11} = {e}_{0}
$$

$$
{e}_{12} = \frac{{e}_{60} - {e}_{120}}{\sqrt{3}} \tag{4. 55}
$$

$$
{e}_{22} = \frac{2\left( {{e}_{60} + {e}_{120}}\right) - {e}_{0}}{3}
$$

根据广义胡克定律, 计算地应力的表示式为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{33} \tag{4. 56}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0
$$

值得注意的是,式中 ${e}_{33}$ 无值,所以很多人将其认为是零,如此,式 (4.56) 成为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{33} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22}}\right) \tag{4. 57}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0
$$

这实际上相当于 ${x}_{3}$ 轴方向上的应变完全被限制住. 但实际情况并非如此,因此有必要作如下讨论.

## 1. 水平应力远大于竖直应力的场合

对水平应力远大于竖直应力的区域,作为近似计算,可视 ${\sigma }_{33}$ 为零,此时,广义胡克定律成为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
0 = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{33} \tag{4. 58}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0
$$

由该式可知, ${e}_{33}$ 不为零,同时可求.

## 2. 水平应力与竖直应力成比例的场合

对地应力实测资料较多的区域, 如冰岛、南非、日本、美国以及我国三峡等部分地区, 可借助于现有水平应力与竖直应力的比值关系进行计算, 当设其比值关系为 $\gamma$ 时,方程式成为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
\frac{\left( {{\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22}}\right) \gamma }{2} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{33}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0 \tag{4. 59}
$$

此时, ${e}_{33}$ 可求.

## 3. 地球表面开放、密度函数已知的场合

对应大部分地区,由于地球表面的开放性,当密度函数为 $\rho \left( {x}_{3}\right)$ 时,广义胡克定律成为

$$
{\sigma }_{11} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{11}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{22} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{22}
$$

$$
{\int }_{0}^{h}\rho \left( {x}_{3}\right) g\mathrm{\;d}{x}_{3} = \lambda \left( {{e}_{11} + {e}_{22} + {e}_{33}}\right) + {2\mu }{e}_{33}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{12} = {2\mu }{e}_{12}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{23} = {\sigma }_{31} = 0 \tag{4. 60}
$$

式中, $g$ 为重力加速度, $h$ 为测点深度. 该式仍然是一个确定的可求方程.

由此可见, 在地球表层上使用广义胡克定律时, 应根据不同情况分别予以处理, 不可千篇一律.

## 二、二维测量之三维地应力主轴旋转问题的理论计算

由前面的讨论可知,通过平面测量,可求出应力张量 ${\sigma }_{ji}$ . 利用求解主应力的特征方程式

$$
{\sigma }^{3} - {J}_{1}{\sigma }^{2} + {J}_{2}\sigma - {J}_{3} = 0 \tag{4. {61}\mathrm{a}}
$$

式中,

$$
{J}_{1} = {\sigma }_{11} + {\sigma }_{22} + {\sigma }_{33}
$$

$$
{J}_{2} = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {\sigma }_{11} & {\sigma }_{12} \\ {\sigma }_{21} & {\sigma }_{22} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {\sigma }_{22} & {\sigma }_{23} \\ {\sigma }_{32} & {\sigma }_{33} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {\sigma }_{33} & {\sigma }_{31} \\ {\sigma }_{13} & {\sigma }_{11} \end{array}\right|
$$

$$
{J}_{3} = \left| \begin{array}{lll} {\sigma }_{11} & {\sigma }_{21} & {\sigma }_{31} \\ {\sigma }_{12} & {\sigma }_{22} & {\sigma }_{32} \\ {\sigma }_{13} & {\sigma }_{23} & {\sigma }_{33} \end{array}\right| \tag{4. {61}\mathrm{\;b}}
$$

可求出主应力值 ${\sigma }_{1}\text{、}{\sigma }_{2}\text{、}{\sigma }_{3}$ ,将其代入

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{matrix} \left( {{\sigma }_{11} - \sigma }\right) & {\sigma }_{21} & {\sigma }_{31} \\ {\sigma }_{12} & \left( {{\sigma }_{22} - \sigma }\right) & {\sigma }_{32} \\ {\sigma }_{13} & {\sigma }_{23} & \left( {{\sigma }_{33} - \sigma }\right) \end{matrix}\right\rbrack = 0 \tag{4.62}
$$

便可求出 ${\sigma }_{1}\text{、}{\sigma }_{2}\text{、}{\sigma }_{3}$ 对应的方向 (称主方向) $\left( {{n}_{1},{n}_{2},{n}_{3}}\right) \text{、}\left( {{n}_{1}^{\prime },{n}_{2}^{\prime },{n}_{3}^{\prime }}\right) \text{、}\left( {{n}_{1}^{\prime \prime },{n}_{2}^{\prime \prime },{n}_{3}^{\prime \prime }}\right)$ . 因此, 根据平面地应力测量, 可以决定地应力主轴的大小和方向.
