分别为速度函数与加速度函数,我们通常把 ${u}_{1}\left( {\Xi \mid k}\right) \text{、}{\dot{u}}_{1}\left( {\Xi \mid k}\right) \text{、}{\ddot{u}}_{1}\left( {\Xi \mid k}\right)$ 分别称为位移型、速度型、加速度型子波函数.

瑞克又引进母函数

$$
{\Psi }_{n}\left( \Xi \right) = \int {P}_{n}\left( \Xi \right) \mathrm{d}T
$$

提出级数解可由 ${\Psi }_{n}\left( \Xi \right)$ 表达,进而得出母函数的一系列关系式.

如果所传播的波是球面波,则上述解的公式中 $k$ 将变为传播距离 $r$ 相应的数值,径向距离 $R = \frac{{\omega }_{0}r}{v}$ . 其解为

$$
{u}_{1} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{\left( \frac{2}{R}\right) }^{\left( {n + 4}\right) /2}{\Psi }_{n}^{\prime }\left( \Xi \right)
$$

$$
{u}_{2} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{\left( \frac{2}{R}\right) }^{\left( {n + 5}\right) /2}{\Psi }_{n}^{2}\left( \Xi \right)
$$

$$
{\dot{u}}_{1} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{\left( \frac{2}{R}\right) }^{\left( {n + 6}\right) /2}{\Psi }_{n}^{3}\left( \Xi \right)
$$

式中

$$
\Xi = \frac{T - R}{{\left( R/2\right) }^{1/2}}
$$

上式结果图示于图 9-22, 该图上的四项分别为母函数、位移子波函数、速度子波函数和加速度子波函数.

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_222_347_541_1063_1205_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_222_347_541_1063_1205_0-20241011170328-tjjje9h.jpg)

图 9-22

1947 年, 美国实验地震队在科罗拉多州 (Colorado) 的莱蒙 (Limon) 地区作了井中观测上述级数解与实际地震子波比较的实验. 这里仅举该实验的一个结果作比较. 这个实测记录是在井下 ${250.71}\mathrm{\;m}$ 处得到的,地面震源深度为 ${76.25}\mathrm{\;m}$ ,偏移距 ${15.25}\mathrm{\;m}$ . 参见图 9-23,这是一个速度型子波记录. 其中实线为实际子波记录, 虚线为 $V\left( {u \mid {25}}\right)$ 子波波形. 即径向数值距 $R$ 取 25, 由公式

$$
{\dot{u}}_{1} = {\left( \frac{2}{R}\right) }^{5/2}V\left( {\Xi \mid R}\right)
$$

![01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_223_226_230_430_398_0.jpg](assets/01927ac2-8a33-7256-99e5-7e8e171f46c5_223_226_230_430_398_0-20241011170328-c3sb310.jpg)

图 9-23

式中

$$
\Xi = \frac{T - R}{{\left( R/2\right) }^{1/2}}
$$

可见, 两者之间的拟合直到第二个弯曲点都是很好的. 从频谱分布也可以证明这一点. 这表明瑞克理论得到的子波函数具有实际意义.

## 习题与参考答案

1. 如何理解介质的蠕变与应力弛豫?
2. 用力学模式描述黏弹体的基本思想与基本原则是什么?
3. 简单线性黏弹体的本构关系如何?
4. 试述品质因数 $Q$ 的物理意义.
5. 试总结弹性波与黏弹波的异同点与传播特性.
6. 对于各向同性的黏弹波, 试导出在一维情况下波动方程. 进一步对平面纵波导出传播速度与衰减系数表达式.

答案: 对于伏各特体

$$
\rho \ddot{{u}_{i}} = \left( {\lambda + \mu }\right) \frac{{\partial }^{2}{u}_{j}}{\partial {u}_{i}\partial {u}_{j}} + \left( {{\lambda }^{\prime } + {\mu }^{\prime }}\right) \frac{{\partial }^{2}{u}_{j}}{\partial {x}_{i}\partial {x}_{j}} + \mu {\nabla }^{\prime 2}{u}_{i} + {\mu }^{\prime }{\nabla }^{2}{\dot{u}}_{i},
$$

$$
v = {\left( \frac{\lambda + {2\mu }}{\rho }\right) }^{1/2},\;r = \frac{{\omega }^{2}\left( {{\lambda }^{\prime } + 2{\mu }^{\prime }}\right) }{{2\rho }{v}^{3}}
$$

7. 本章列举了黏弹波在低频 $\left( {0 \sim {80}\mathrm{\;{Hz}}}\right)$ 带的传播变化资料. 请给出它的物理解释. 比较黏弹波在不同频带传播特性, 并加以物理分析.
8. 以速度 $C$ 沿 ${x}_{1}$ 轴正方向传播的一平面设 $\delta \left( {t - {x}_{1}/v}\right)$ ,它在 ${x}_{1} = 0$ 进入一衰减介质. 在距离 ${x}_{1}$ ,衰减波的脉冲形态为

$$
p\left( {{x}_{1}, t}\right) = \frac{1}{2\pi }{\int }_{-\infty }^{\infty }\exp \left\lbrack \frac{-\left| \omega \right| {x}_{1}}{2CQ}\right\rbrack \exp \left\lbrack {\mathrm{i}\omega \left( {\frac{{x}_{1}}{C} - \mathrm{i}}\right) }\right\rbrack \mathrm{d}\omega
$$

试在 $Q$ 为常数的情况,讨论 $p\left( {{x}_{1}, t}\right)$ 的形状. 又若 $Q$ 为偶函数,即 $Q\left( {-\omega }\right) =$ $Q\left( \omega \right)$ ,但无频散,再讨论 $p\left( {{x}_{1}, t}\right)$ 的形状.

9. 试说明 N. H. Ricker 的研究黏弹性介质中的地震波的方法.

## F. 2 张量简介

在物理中, 为了表示空间某点的物理状态和性质, 常常引入标量和矢量. 标量是只有数值大小而无方向的量, 并只有一个分量, 如温度、密度等. 矢量是有大小和方向的量, 如速度、加速度、电场强度等. 矢量有 3 个分量. 然而在实际问题中发现, 只用标量、矢量还不足以描述某些物理量的特征, 如连续体的内应力, 它是面力. 任一面上的力, 不仅与面积的大小有关, 而且与面积的取向有关. 这样一种性质的力用矢量就不能完全表示它的性质. 诸如此类, 就迫使人们扩大原来标量、矢量的概念, 引入一个新的量一张量来描述某些量的性质. 引入张量的概念需要注意以下两点: 首先, 应使它保持原有标量和矢量的主要性质; 其次, 应把标量和矢量包括在新定义的范围之内.

矢量的一个重要性质是当坐标轴旋转时矢量的长度保持不变. 为了将这一性质表达成数学形式, 我们需要研究坐标轴旋转时空间一点的坐标变换关系, 并从矢量长度不变性去得出这种变换满足的条件. 在此基础上将矢量定义加以推广, 就得到张量定义. 本书定义的张量限于直角坐标系, 相应的张量称为笛卡儿张量.

## F. 2.1 坐标变换

设两个直角坐标系具有相同原点. 空间一点 $P$ ,在两个坐标系中的位置分别为 $\left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3}}\right)$ 和 $\left( {{x}_{1}^{\prime },{x}_{2}^{\prime }{x}_{3}^{\prime }}\right) .{x}_{i}^{\prime }\left( {i = 1,2,3}\right)$ 坐标系可看成是由 ${x}_{j}$ 坐标系旋转而成. 设 ${\alpha }_{ij} = \cos \left( {{x}_{i}^{\prime },{x}_{j}}\right)$ 表示 ${x}_{i}^{\prime }$ 轴与 ${x}_{j}$ 轴夹角的方向余弦. 则新旧坐标的变换关系为

$$
{x}_{i}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{ij}{x}_{j},\;i, j = 1,2,3 \tag{F. 1}
$$

或者

$$
{x}_{1}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{11}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{12}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{13}{x}_{3}
$$

$$
{x}_{2}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{21}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{22}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{23}{x}_{3} \tag{F. 2}
$$

$$
{x}_{3}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{31}{x}_{1} + {\alpha }_{32}{x}_{2} + {\alpha }_{33}{x}_{3}
$$

它的矩阵形式为

$$
\left\lbrack \begin{array}{l} {x}_{1}^{\prime } \\ {x}_{2}^{\prime } \\ {x}_{3}^{\prime } \end{array}\right\rbrack = \left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} {\alpha }_{11} & {\alpha }_{12} & {\alpha }_{13} \\ {\alpha }_{21} & {\alpha }_{22} & {\alpha }_{23} \\ {\alpha }_{31} & {\alpha }_{32} & {\alpha }_{33} \end{array}\right\rbrack \left\lbrack \begin{array}{l} {x}_{1} \\ {x}_{2} \\ {x}_{3} \end{array}\right\rbrack \tag{F. 3}
$$

式(F. 3) 的反变换可写成

$$
{x}_{i} = {\alpha }_{ji}{x}_{j}^{\prime },\;i, j = 1,2,3 \tag{F. 4}
$$

从长度不变性 ${x}_{i}{x}_{i} = {x}_{j}^{\prime }{x}_{j}^{\prime } = {x}_{i}^{\prime }{x}_{i}^{\prime } = {x}_{j}{x}_{j}$ 可得 ${\alpha }_{ij}$ 的下述性质,即

$$
{\alpha }_{ij}{\alpha }_{ik} = {\delta }_{jk} \tag{F. 5}
$$

$$
{\alpha }_{ji}{\alpha }_{ki} = {\delta }_{jk}
$$

具有这种性质的变换称为线性正交变换.

## F. 2.2 定义

零阶张量:一量 $\varphi$ ,它只有 1 个分量,当坐标按照式 (F. 1) 变换时,它保持恒定, 则 $\varphi$ 称为标量或零阶张量.

一阶张量: 设量 $A$ 有 3 个分量 ${A}_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,3}\right)$ ,当坐标按式 (F. 1) 变换时,它按下式变换:

$$
{A}_{i}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{ji}{A}_{j} \tag{F. 6}
$$

则 ${A}_{i}$ 称为一阶张量或矢量.

二阶张量: 设有一量 $B$ ,它有 9 个分量 ${B}_{ij}\left( {i, j = 1,2,3}\right)$ 当坐标按式 (F. 1) 变换, ${B}_{ij}$ 按下式变换:

$$
{B}_{ij}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{il}{\alpha }_{jm}{B}_{lm} \tag{F. 7}
$$

则 ${B}_{ij}$ 称为二阶张量.

三阶张量: 设有一量 $c$ ,它有 ${3}^{3} = {27}$ 个分量 ${c}_{ijk} = \left( {i, j, k = 1,2,3}\right)$ ,当坐标按式(F. 1) 变换时, 它按下式变换:

$$
{c}_{ijk} = {\alpha }_{ir}{\alpha }_{je}{\alpha }_{kl}{c}_{rel} \tag{F. 8}
$$

则 ${c}_{ijk}$ 称为三阶张量.

$n$ 阶张量: 设一量有 ${3}^{n}$ 个分量,当坐标按式(F. 1)变换时,它按下式变换:

$$
{e}_{{ijkl}\cdots n} = {\alpha }_{ir}{\alpha }_{je}{\alpha }_{ki}\cdots {\alpha }_{ny}{e}_{{rki}\cdots y} \tag{F. 9}
$$

则 ${e}_{{ijkl}\cdots n}$ 称为 $n$ 阶张量.

## F. 2.3 性质

从张量定义可得张量的如下性质:

(1)两个阶数相同的张量可以相加或相减,所得结果与原张量同阶. 设 ${d}_{ij}$ 和 ${b}_{ij}$ 为二阶张量,则

$$
{c}_{ij} = {d}_{ij} + {b}_{ij} \tag{F. 10}
$$

(2)两个一阶张量 ${d}_{i}$ 和 ${d}_{j}$ ,它的乘积定义为

$$
{c}_{ij} = {d}_{i}{b}_{j} \tag{F. 11}
$$

由于

$$
{c}_{ij}^{\prime } = {d}_{i}^{\prime }{b}_{j}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{li}{\alpha }_{jm}{d}_{l}{b}_{m} \tag{F. 12}
$$

可见两个一阶张量相乘, 结果为二阶张量. 同样, 一阶张量与二阶张量的积为三阶张量. 推而广之, 乘积后张量阶数等于相乘张量阶数相加.

(3)对称张量及反对称张量: 设张量 ${d}_{ij}$ ,当 $i, j$ 互换后相等,即 ${d}_{ij} = {d}_{ji}$ ,则此张量称为对称张量. 当 ${d}_{ij} = - {d}_{ji}$ ,则 ${d}_{ij}$ 称为反对称张量. 写成矩阵形式,对称张量 ${T}_{ij}$ 可表示为

$$
\mathbf{T} = \left\lbrack \begin{array}{lll} {T}_{11} & {T}_{12} & {T}_{13} \\ {T}_{12} & {T}_{22} & {T}_{23} \\ {T}_{13} & {T}_{23} & {T}_{33} \end{array}\right\rbrack \tag{F. 13}
$$

反对称张量 ${T}_{ij}$ 可表示为

$$
\mathbf{T} = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} {T}_{11} & {T}_{12} & {T}_{13} \\ - {T}_{12} & {T}_{22} & {T}_{23} \\ - {T}_{13} & - {T}_{23} & {T}_{33} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack \tag{F. 14}
$$

任一二阶张量可以表示成对称张量与反对称张量之和. 例如,

$$
{T}_{ij} = \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {{T}_{ij} + {T}_{ji}}\right\rbrack + \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {{T}_{ij} - {T}_{ji}}\right\rbrack = {A}_{ij} + {B}_{ij} \tag{F. 15}
$$

式中, ${A}_{ij} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{T}_{ij} + {T}_{ji}}\right)$ 为对称张量, ${B}_{ij} = \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack {{T}_{ij} - {T}_{ji}}\right\rbrack$ 为反对称张量.

(4)张量的缩阶: 三阶张量 ${d}_{ijk}$ ,令其中两个指标相等,称为张量缩阶. 缩阶后张量为 ${d}_{ikk}$ ,它是一阶张量. 任一张量缩阶后阶数减少二阶.

(5) 张量不变量: 任一二阶张量 ${T}_{ij}$ ,有 3 个不变量 ${T}_{ii},{T}_{ij}{T}_{ji},{T}_{ij}{T}_{jk}{T}_{ki}$ . 即在坐标按式(F. 1)变换时它们保持恒定, 或者写成

$$
{T}_{ii} = {T}_{ii}^{\prime }
$$

$$
{T}_{ij}{T}_{ji} = {T}_{ij}^{\prime }{T}_{ji}^{\prime } \tag{F. 16}
$$

$$
{T}_{ij}{T}_{jk}{T}_{ki} = {T}_{ij}^{\prime }{T}_{jk}^{\prime }{T}_{ki}^{\prime }
$$

## F. 2.4 张量判别定理

定理 1 设有 ${A}_{j}\text{、}{B}_{i}$ 是一阶张量,假如 ${T}_{ij}$ 与 ${A}_{j}$ 的积满足下列关系:

$$
{B}_{i} = {T}_{ij}{A}_{j} \tag{F. 17}
$$

则 ${T}_{ij}$ 是二阶张量. 其证明如下:

因为

$$
{B}_{i}^{\prime } = {T}_{ij}^{\prime }{A}_{j}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{ik}{B}_{k} = {\alpha }_{ik}{T}_{km}{A}_{m}
$$

且

$$
{A}_{m} = {\alpha }_{nm}{A}_{n}^{\prime }
$$

代入上式右端可得

$$
{T}_{ij}^{\prime }{A}_{j}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{ik}{\alpha }_{nm}{T}_{km}{A}_{n}^{\prime }
$$

此式左端重复指标 $j$ 表示对它求和,故用 $n$ 代换 $j$ 不影响结果,于是有

$$
\left( {{T}_{in}^{\prime } - {\alpha }_{ik}{\alpha }_{nm}{T}_{km}^{\prime }}\right) {A}_{n}^{\prime } = 0
$$

因 ${A}^{\prime } \neq 0$ ,故此可得

$$
{T}_{in}^{\prime } = {\alpha }_{ik}{\alpha }_{nm}{T}_{km}
$$

此式表示 ${T}_{ij}$ 为二阶张量.

定理 2 设 ${A}_{i}\text{、}{B}_{j}$ 是一阶张量. 若 ${T}_{ij}{A}_{i}{B}_{j}$ 是零阶张量,则 ${T}_{ij}$ 是二阶张量. 证明从略.

从张量定义知替代符号 ${\delta }_{ij}$ 是二阶单位张量. 循环符号 ${\delta }_{ijk}$ 是三阶张量.

## F. 3 相似矩阵的特征值

设 $\mathbf{M}$ 表示一矩阵, ${\mathbf{M}}^{-1}$ 表示 $\mathbf{M}$ 的逆矩阵. 当矩阵 $\mathbf{A}$ 与矩阵 $\mathbf{D}$ 满足

$$
\mathbf{D} = {\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\mathbf{{AM}} \tag{F. 18}
$$

关系时,则称 $\mathbf{D}$ 与 $\mathbf{A}$ 是相似的.

若有一线性正交变换

$$
\left( \mathbf{T}\right) = \mathbf{A}\left( x\right) \tag{F. 19}
$$

这里用 () 号表示矢量, 它的分量形式为

$$
{T}_{i} = {A}_{ij}{x}_{j},\;i, j = 1,2,3 \tag{F. 20}
$$

式(F. 20) 可以理解为变换算符作用在矢量 ${x}_{j}$ 上,将矢量 ${x}_{j}$ 变换成矢量 ${T}_{i}$ . 现在我们寻找矢量 ${x}_{j}$ 的某一方向,它在变换时保持方向恒定. 即变换后仍与原来方向平行. 在数学上表示为

$$
\left( T\right) = \lambda \left( x\right)
$$

或

$$
A\left( x\right) = {\lambda I}\left( x\right) \tag{F. 21}
$$

式中, $\lambda$ 为一常数, $I$ 为单位张量. 式(F. 21) 还可写成如下形式:

$$
\left( {A - {\lambda I}}\right) \left( x\right) = 0 \tag{F. 22}
$$

式(F. 22) 是对于 ${x}_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,3}\right)$ 的线性方程组,若使它有非零解. 其系数行列式应为零, 即

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} {\alpha }_{11} - \lambda & {\alpha }_{12} & {\alpha }_{13} \\ {\alpha }_{21} & {\alpha }_{22} - \lambda & {\alpha }_{23} \\ {\alpha }_{31} & {\alpha }_{32} & {\alpha }_{33} - \lambda \end{matrix}\right| = 0
$$

展开后得 $\lambda$ 的三次方程

$$
{\lambda }^{3} - {I}_{1}{\lambda }^{2} + {I}_{2}\lambda - {I}_{3} = 0 \tag{F. 23}
$$

式中

$$
{I}_{1} = {\alpha }_{11} + {\alpha }_{22} + {\alpha }_{33} \tag{F. 24}
$$

$$
{I}_{2} = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {\alpha }_{11} & {\alpha }_{12} \\ {\alpha }_{21} & {\alpha }_{22} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {\alpha }_{22} & {\alpha }_{23} \\ {\alpha }_{32} & {\alpha }_{33} \end{array}\right| + \left| \begin{array}{ll} {\alpha }_{33} & {\alpha }_{31} \\ {\alpha }_{13} & {\alpha }_{11} \end{array}\right| \tag{F. 25}
$$

$$
{I}_{3} = \left| \begin{array}{lll} {\alpha }_{11} & {\alpha }_{12} & {\alpha }_{13} \\ {\alpha }_{21} & {\alpha }_{22} & {\alpha }_{23} \\ {\alpha }_{31} & {\alpha }_{32} & {\alpha }_{33} \end{array}\right| \tag{F. 26}
$$

在一般情况下,有 3 个根,即 ${\lambda }_{1}\text{、}{\lambda }_{2}\text{、}{\lambda }_{3}$ 它们称为本征方程 (F. 23) 的特征值. 对每一个 $\lambda$ ,代入方程 (F. 22) 可得一组 ${x}_{i}$ ,它们相应于一个矢量,称特征矢量. 将每个矢量的分量作为矩阵 $\mathbf{M}$ 的行即得一方阵 $\mathbf{M}$ ( 3 个矢量,每个矢量 3 个分量). 特征值 $\lambda$ 构成一对角矩阵, 即

$$
\mathbf{D} = \left\lbrack \begin{matrix} {\lambda }_{1} & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & {\lambda }_{2} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & {\lambda }_{3} \end{matrix}\right\rbrack \tag{F. 27}
$$

利用对角矩阵可以把方程组写成矩阵方程,于是式(F. 21)可写成

$$
\mathbf{{AM}} = \mathbf{{MD}} \tag{F. 28}
$$

用 ${\mathbf{M}}^{-1}$ 左乘式(F. 28)得

$$
{\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\mathbf{{AM}} = \mathbf{D} \tag{F. 29}
$$

方程 (F. 29) 说明 $\mathbf{D}$ 与 ${\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\mathbf{{AM}}$ 满足式 (F. 18). 相似矩阵有一重要性质,就是它们的特征相同. 为了证明这点,将 ${\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\mathbf{A}\mathbf{M}$ 代替方程 (F. 22) 中的 $\mathbf{A}$ 得

$$
\left| {{\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\mathbf{{AM}} - \lambda \mathbf{I}}\right|
$$

$$
= \left| {\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\right| \left| {\mathbf{A} - \lambda \mathbf{I}}\right| \left| \mathbf{M}\right| \tag{F. 30}
$$

$$
= \left| {\mathbf{A} - \lambda \mathbf{I}}\right|
$$

可见 ${\mathbf{M}}^{-1}\mathbf{A}\mathbf{M}$ 的特征方程与 $\mathbf{A}$ 的特征方程是相同的. 它的特征值也是相同的. 这说明 ${\lambda }_{1}\text{、}{\lambda }_{2}\text{、}{\lambda }_{3}$ 不随线性变换而改变,即它是不变量.

由于 ${\lambda }_{1}\text{、}{\lambda }_{2}\text{、}{\lambda }_{3}$ 是方程 (F. 22) 的 3 个根,应有

$$
\left( {\lambda - {\lambda }_{1}}\right) \left( {\lambda - {\lambda }_{2}}\right) \left( {\lambda - {\lambda }_{3}}\right) = 0 \tag{F. 31}
$$

将式(F. 31)展开并与式(F. 25) 比较可得

$$
{I}_{1} = {\lambda }_{1} + {\lambda }_{2} + {\lambda }_{3} \tag{F. 32}
$$

$$
{I}_{2} = {\lambda }_{1}{\lambda }_{2} + {\lambda }_{2}{\lambda }_{3} + {\lambda }_{3}{\lambda }_{1} \tag{F. 33}
$$

$$
{I}_{3} = {\lambda }_{1}{\lambda }_{2}{\lambda }_{3} \tag{F. 34}
$$

既然 ${\lambda }_{1}\text{、}{\lambda }_{2}\text{、}{\lambda }_{3}$ 为不变量,那么推知 ${I}_{1}\text{、}{I}_{2}\text{、}{I}_{3}$ 也是不变量.

## F. 4 曲线坐标中的运算公式

## F. 4. 1 柱坐标系

$$
\operatorname{grad}\varphi = \frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial r}{e}_{r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial \theta }{e}_{\theta } + \frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial z}{e}_{z} \tag{F. 35}
$$

$$
\mathrm{{dlv}}A = \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial }{\partial r}\left( {r{A}_{r}}\right) + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {A}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{\partial A}{\partial z} \tag{F. 36}
$$

$$
\operatorname{rot}A = \left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {A}_{z}}{\partial \theta } - \frac{\partial {A}_{\theta }}{\partial z}}\right) {e}_{r} + \left( {\frac{\partial {A}_{r}}{\partial z} - \frac{\partial {A}_{z}}{\partial r}}\right) {e}_{\theta } + \left\lbrack {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial }{\partial r}\left( {r{A}_{\theta }}\right) - \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {A}_{r}}{\partial \theta }}\right\rbrack {e}_{z} \tag{F. 37}
$$

$$
{\nabla }^{2}\varphi = \frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi }{\partial {r}^{2}} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial r} + \frac{1}{{r}^{2}}\frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi }{\partial {\theta }^{2}} + \frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi }{\partial {z}^{2}} \tag{F. 38}
$$

$$
{\nabla }^{2}A = \left( {{\nabla }^{2}{A}_{r} - \frac{A}{{r}^{2}} - \frac{2}{{r}^{2}}\frac{\partial {A}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta }}\right) {e}_{r} + \left( {{\nabla }^{2}{A}_{\theta } + \frac{{A}_{\theta }}{{r}^{2}} + \frac{2}{{r}^{2}}\frac{\partial A}{\partial \theta }}\right) {e}_{\theta } + {\nabla }^{2}{A}_{z}{e}_{z} \tag{F. 39}
$$

应变分量

$$
{e}_{rr} = \frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r},\;{e}_{\theta \theta } = \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}
$$

$$
{e}_{zz} = \frac{\partial {u}_{z}}{\partial z},\;{e}_{r\theta } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial \theta } + \frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial r} - \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}}\right) \tag{F. 40}
$$

$$
{e}_{zr} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{z}}{\partial r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial z}}\right)
$$

$$
{e}_{\theta z} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial z} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{z}}{\partial \theta }}\right)
$$

广义胡克定律

$$
{\sigma }_{ji} = \lambda {e}_{kk}{\delta }_{ji} + {2\mu }{e}_{ji} \tag{F. 41}
$$

${\sigma }_{ji}\text{、}{e}_{ij}$ 角标 $i\text{、}j$ 分别取 $1\text{、}2\text{、}3$ 时各对应 $r\text{、}\theta \text{、}z$ .

应力分量

$$
{\sigma }_{rr} = \lambda \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}}\right) + {2\mu }\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{\theta \theta } = \lambda \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}}\right) + {2\mu }\left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{zz} = \lambda \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}}\right) + {2\mu }\frac{\partial {u}_{z}}{\partial z} \tag{F. 42}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{r\theta } = \mu \left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial \theta } + \frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial r} + \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{zr} = \mu \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{z}}{\partial r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial z}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{\theta z} = \mu \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial z} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{z}}{\partial \theta }}\right)
$$

## F. 4.2 球坐标系

$$
\operatorname{grad}\varphi = \frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial r}{e}_{r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial \theta }{e}_{\theta } + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial \alpha }{e}_{\alpha } \tag{F. 43}
$$

$$
\operatorname{dlv}A = \frac{1}{{r}^{2}}\frac{\partial }{\partial r}\left( {{r}^{2}{A}_{r}}\right) + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial }{\partial \theta }\left( {{A}_{\theta }\sin \theta }\right) + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {A}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } \tag{F. 44}
$$

$$
\operatorname{rot}A = \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\left\lbrack {\frac{\partial }{\partial \theta }\left( {{A}_{\alpha }\sin \theta }\right) - \frac{\partial {A}_{\theta }}{\partial \alpha }}\right\rbrack {e}_{r} + \left\lbrack {\frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {A}_{r}}{\partial \alpha } - \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial }{\partial r}\left( {r{A}_{\alpha }}\right) }\right\rbrack {e}_{\theta }
$$

$$
+ \frac{1}{r}\left\lbrack {\frac{\partial }{\partial r}\left( {r{A}_{\theta }}\right) - \frac{\partial {A}_{r}}{\partial \theta }}\right\rbrack {e}_{\alpha } \tag{F. 45}
$$

$$
{\nabla }^{2}\varphi = \frac{1}{{r}^{2}}\frac{\partial }{\partial r}\left( {{r}^{2}\frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial r}}\right) + \frac{1}{{r}^{2}\sin \theta }\frac{\partial }{\partial \theta }\left( {\sin \theta \frac{\partial \varphi }{\partial \theta }}\right) + \frac{1}{{r}^{2}{\sin }^{2}\theta }\frac{{\partial }^{2}\varphi }{\partial {\alpha }^{2}} \tag{F. 46}
$$

$$
{\nabla }^{2}A = \left\lbrack {{\nabla }^{2}{A}_{r} - \frac{2}{{r}^{2}}{A}_{r} - \frac{2}{{r}^{2}\sin \theta }\frac{\partial }{\partial \theta }\left( {{A}_{\theta }\sin \theta }\right) - \frac{2}{{r}^{2}\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {A}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha }}\right\rbrack {e}_{r}
$$

$$
+ \left\lbrack {{\nabla }^{2}{A}_{\theta } - \frac{{A}_{\theta }}{{r}^{2}\sin \theta } + \frac{2}{{r}^{2}}\frac{\partial A}{\partial \theta } - \frac{2}{{r}^{2}}\frac{\cos \theta }{{\sin }^{2}\theta }\frac{\partial {A}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha }}\right\rbrack {e}_{\theta }
$$

$$
+ \left\lbrack {{\nabla }^{2}{A}_{\alpha } - \frac{{A}_{\alpha }}{{r}^{2}{\sin }^{2}\theta } + \frac{2}{{r}^{2}\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {A}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } + \frac{2\cos \theta }{{r}^{2}{\sin }^{2}\theta }\frac{\partial {A}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha }}\right\rbrack {e}_{\alpha } \tag{F. 47}
$$

应变分量

$$
{e}_{rr} = \frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r},\;{e}_{\theta \theta } = \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}
$$

$$
{e}_{\alpha \alpha } = \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r} + \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}\cot \theta
$$

$$
{e}_{r\alpha } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial \alpha } - \frac{{u}_{\alpha }}{r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial r}}\right) \tag{F. 48}
$$

$$
{e}_{r\theta } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial \theta } - \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial r}}\right)
$$

$$
{e}_{\alpha \theta } = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \theta } - \frac{{u}_{\alpha }}{r}\cot \theta + \frac{1}{r\sin \alpha }\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \alpha }}\right)
$$

广义胡克定律

$$
{\sigma }_{ji} = \lambda {e}_{kk}{\delta }_{ji} + {2\mu }{e}_{ji}
$$

${\sigma }_{ji}\text{、}{e}_{ji}$ 中 $i, j = 1,2,3$ 时,相应角标对应 $r,\theta ,\alpha$ .

应力张量分量

$$
{\sigma }_{rr} = \lambda \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{2{u}_{r}}{r} + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } + \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}\cot \theta }\right) + {2\mu }\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{\theta \theta } = \lambda \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{2{u}_{r}}{r} + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } + \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}\cot \theta }\right) + {2\mu }\left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{\theta \alpha } = \lambda \left( {\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial r} + \frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \theta } + \frac{2{u}_{r}}{r} + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } + \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}\cot \theta }\right)
$$

$$
+ {2\mu }\left( {\frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \alpha } + \frac{{u}_{r}}{r} + \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r}\cot \theta }\right) \tag{F. 49}
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{r\alpha } = \mu \left( {\frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial \alpha } - \frac{{u}_{\alpha }}{r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial r}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{r\theta } = \mu \left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{r}}{\partial \theta } - \frac{{u}_{\theta }}{r} + \frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial r}}\right)
$$

$$
{\sigma }_{\alpha \theta } = \mu \left( {\frac{1}{r}\frac{\partial {u}_{\alpha }}{\partial \theta } - \frac{{u}_{\alpha }}{r}\cot \theta + \frac{1}{r\sin \theta }\frac{\partial {u}_{\theta }}{\partial \alpha }}\right)
$$

说明: 曲线坐标系下的应变张量及应力张量公式之导出, 过程繁冗, 故此处仅给出其结果.
